Ekamantaṃ, ṭhito kho brahmā sahampati bhagavantaṃ etadavoca – ‘‘kokāliko, bhante, bhikkhu kālaṅkato; kālaṅkato ca, bhante, kokāliko bhikkhu padumaṃ nirayaṃ upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’’ti. Idamavoca brahmā sahampati; idaṃ vatvā bhagavantaṃ abhivādetvā padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyi.

Atha kho bhagavā tassā rattiyā accayena bhikkhū āmantesi – ‘‘imaṃ, bhikkhave, rattiṃ brahmā sahampati abhikkantāya rattiyā…pe… idamavoca, bhikkhave, brahmā sahampati, idaṃ vatvā maṃ padakkhiṇaṃ katvā tatthevantaradhāyī’’ti.

Evaṃ vutte, aññataro bhikkhu bhagavantaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0126" /> etadavoca – ‘‘kīvadīghaṃ nu kho, bhante, padume niraye āyuppamāṇa’’nti? ‘‘Dīghaṃ kho, bhikkhu, padume niraye āyuppamāṇaṃ; taṃ na sukaraṃ saṅkhātuṃ ettakāni vassāni iti vā ettakāni vassasatāni iti vā ettakāni vassasahassāni <pb ed="M" n="0.0381" /> iti vā ettakāni vassasatasahassāni iti vā’’ti. ‘‘Sakkā pana, bhante, upamā <note>upamaṃ (sī. syā. ka.)</note> kātu’’nti? ‘‘Sakkā, bhikkhū’’ti bhagavā avoca –

‘‘Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho; tato puriso vassasatassa vassasatassa accayena ekamekaṃ tilaṃ uddhareyya. Khippataraṃ kho so bhikkhu vīsatikhāriko kosalako tilavāho <pb ed="T" n="0.0461" /> iminā upakkamena parikkhayaṃ pariyādānaṃ gaccheyya, natveva eko abbudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati abbudā nirayā evameko nirabbudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati nirabbudā nirayā evameko ababo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ababā nirayā evameko ahaho nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati ahahā nirayā evameko aṭaṭo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati aṭaṭā nirayā evameko kumudo nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati kumudā nirayā evameko sogandhiko nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati sogandhikā nirayā evameko uppalako nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati uppalakā nirayā evameko puṇḍarīko nirayo. Seyyathāpi, bhikkhu, vīsati puṇḍarīkā nirayā evameko padumo nirayo. Padumaṃ kho pana bhikkhu nirayaṃ kokāliko bhikkhu upapanno sāriputtamoggallānesu cittaṃ āghātetvā’’ti. Idamavoca bhagavā, idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§662.</p>

```
‘‘Purisassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0183" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0127" /> hi jātassa, kuṭhārī <note>kudhārī (ka.)</note> jāyate mukhe;
```

```
Yāya chindati attānaṃ, bālo dubbhāsitaṃ bhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§663.</p>

```
‘‘Yo nindiyaṃ pasaṃsati, taṃ vā nindati yo pasaṃsiyo;
```

```
Vicināti mukhena so kaliṃ, kalinā <pb ed="T" n="0.0462" /> tena sukhaṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§664.</p>

```
‘‘Appamatto <pb ed="M" n="0.0382" /> ayaṃ kali, yo akkhesu dhanaparājayo;
```

```
Sabbassāpi sahāpi attanā, ayameva mahattaro <note>mahantakaro (sī.)</note> kali;
```

```
Yo sugatesu manaṃ padosaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§665.</p>

```
‘‘Sataṃ sahassānaṃ nirabbudānaṃ, chattiṃsati pañca ca abbudāni <note>abbudānaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Yamariyagarahī nirayaṃ upeti, vācaṃ manañca paṇidhāya pāpakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§666.</p>

```
‘‘Abhūtavādī nirayaṃ upeti, yo vāpi katvā na karomicāha;
```

```
Ubhopi te pecca samā bhavanti, nihīnakammā manujā parattha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§667.</p>

```
‘‘Yo appaduṭṭhassa narassa dussati, suddhassa posassa anaṅgaṇassa;
```

```
Tameva bālaṃ pacceti pāpaṃ, sukhumo rajo paṭivātaṃva khitto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§668.</p>

```
‘‘Yo lobhaguṇe anuyutto, so vacasā paribhāsati aññe;
```

```
Asaddho <pb ed="P" n="0.0128" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0463" /> kadariyo avadaññū, macchari pesuṇiyaṃ <note>pesuṇiyasmiṃ (bahūsu)</note> anuyutto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§669.</p>

```
‘‘Mukhadugga vibhūta anariya, bhūnahu <note>bhunahata (syā. ka.)</note> pāpaka dukkaṭakāri;
```

```
Purisanta kalī avajāta, mā bahubhāṇidha nerayikosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§670.</p>

```
‘‘Rajamākirasī <pb ed="M" n="0.0383" /> ahitāya, sante garahasi kibbisakārī;
```

```
Bahūni duccaritāni caritvā, gacchasi kho papataṃ cirarattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§671.</p>

```
‘‘Na hi nassati kassaci kammaṃ, eti hataṃ labhateva suvāmi;
```

```
Dukkhaṃ mando paraloke, attani passati kibbisakārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§672.</p>

```
‘‘Ayosaṅkusamāhataṭṭhānaṃ<pb ed="V" n="0.0184" />, tiṇhadhāramayasūlamupeti;
```

```
Atha <pb ed="P" n="0.0129" /> tattaayoguḷasannibhaṃ, bhojanamatthi tathā patirūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§673.</p>

```
‘‘Na hi vaggu vadanti vadantā, nābhijavanti na tāṇamupenti;
```

```
Aṅgāre <pb ed="T" n="0.0464" /> santhate sayanti <note>senti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, ginisampajjalitaṃ pavisanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§674.</p>

```
‘‘Jālena ca onahiyāna, tattha hananti ayomayakuṭebhi <note>ayomayakūṭehi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Andhaṃva timisamāyanti, taṃ vitatañhi yathā mahikāyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§675.</p>

```
‘‘Atha lohamayaṃ pana kumbhiṃ, ginisampajjalitaṃ pavisanti;
```

```
Paccanti hi tāsu cirarattaṃ, agginisamāsu <note>ginissamāsu (ka.)</note> samuppilavāte.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§676.</p>

```
‘‘Atha pubbalohitamisse, tattha kiṃ paccati kibbisakārī;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0130" /> disakaṃ <note>disataṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> adhiseti, tattha kilissati samphusamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§677.</p>

```
‘‘Puḷavāvasathe <pb ed="M" n="0.0384" /> salilasmiṃ, tattha kiṃ paccati kibbisakārī;
```

```
Gantuṃ na hi tīramapatthi, sabbasamā hi samantakapallā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§678.</p>

```
‘‘Asipattavanaṃ pana tiṇhaṃ, taṃ pavisanti samucchidagattā;
```

```
Jivhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0465" /> balisena gahetvā, ārajayārajayā vihananti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§679.</p>

```
‘‘Atha vetaraṇiṃ pana duggaṃ, tiṇhadhārakhuradhāramupenti;
```

```
Tattha mandā papatanti, pāpakarā pāpāni karitvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§680.</p>

```
‘‘Khādanti <pb ed="P" n="0.0131" /> hi tattha rudante, sāmā sabalā kākolagaṇā ca;
```

```
Soṇā siṅgālā <note>sigālā (sī. pī.)</note> paṭigiddhā <note>paṭigijjhā (syā. pī.)</note>, kulalā vāyasā ca <note>kulalā ca vāyasā (?)</note> vitudanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§681.</p>

```
‘‘Kicchā vatayaṃ idha vutti, yaṃ jano phusati <note>passati (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kibbisakārī;
```

```
Tasmā idha jīvitasese, kiccakaro siyā naro na cappamajje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§682.</p>

```
‘‘Te <pb ed="V" n="0.0185" /> gaṇitā vidūhi tilavāhā, ye padume niraye upanītā;
```

```
Nahutāni hi koṭiyo pañca bhavanti, dvādasa koṭisatāni punaññā <note>panayye (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§683.</p>

```
‘‘Yāva <pb ed="M" n="0.0385" /> dukhā <note>dukkhā (sī. syā.), dukkha (pī. ka.)</note> nirayā idha vuttā, tatthapi tāva ciraṃ vasitabbaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā <pb ed="T" n="0.0466" /> sucipesalasādhuguṇesu, vācaṃ manaṃ satataṃ <note>pakataṃ (syā.)</note> parirakkhe’’ti.
```

Kokālikasuttaṃ dasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 11. Nālakasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§684.</p>

```
Ānandajāte tidasagaṇe patīte, sakkañca indaṃ sucivasane ca deve;
```

```
Dussaṃ gahetvā atiriva thomayante, asito isi addasa divāvihāre.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§685.</p>

```
Disvāna <pb ed="P" n="0.0132" /> deve muditamane udagge, cittiṃ karitvāna idamavoca <note>karitvā idamavocāsi (sī.)</note> tattha;
```

```
‘‘Kiṃ devasaṅgho atiriva kalyarūpo, dussaṃ gahetvā ramayatha <note>bhamayatha (sī.)</note> kiṃ paṭicca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§686.</p>

```
‘‘Yadāpi āsī asurehi saṅgamo, jayo surānaṃ asurā parājitā.
```

```
Tadāpi netādiso lomahaṃsano, kimabbhutaṃ daṭṭhu marū pamoditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§687.</p>

```
‘‘Seḷenti gāyanti ca vādayanti ca, bhujāni phoṭenti <note>poṭhenti (sī. pī.), pothenti (ka.)</note> ca naccayanti ca;
```

```
Pucchāmi <pb ed="T" n="0.0467" /> vohaṃ merumuddhavāsine, dhunātha me saṃsayaṃ khippa mārisā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§688.</p>

```
‘‘So <pb ed="M" n="0.0386" /> bodhisatto ratanavaro atulyo, manussaloke hitasukhatthāya <note>hitasukhatāya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jāto;
```

```
Sakyāna gāme janapade lumbineyye, tenamha tuṭṭhā atiriva kalyarūpā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§689.</p>

```
‘‘So sabbasattuttamo aggapuggalo, narāsabho sabbapajānamuttamo;
```

```
Vattessati <pb ed="P" n="0.0133" /> cakkamisivhaye vane, nadaṃva sīho balavā migābhibhū’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§690.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0186" /> saddaṃ sutvā turitamavasarī so, suddhodanassa tada bhavanaṃ upāvisi <note>upāgami (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nisajja tattha idamavocāsi sakye, ‘‘kuhiṃ kumāro ahamapi daṭṭhukāmo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§691.</p>

```
Tato kumāraṃ jalitamiva suvaṇṇaṃ, ukkāmukheva sukusalasampahaṭṭhaṃ <note>sukusalena sampahaṭṭhaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Daddallamānaṃ <note>daddaḷhamānaṃ (ka.)</note> siriyā anomavaṇṇaṃ, dassesu puttaṃ asitavhayassa sakyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§692.</p>

```
Disvā kumāraṃ sikhimiva pajjalantaṃ, tārāsabhaṃva <pb ed="T" n="0.0468" /> nabhasigamaṃ visuddhaṃ;
```

```
Sūriyaṃ tapantaṃ saradarivabbhamuttaṃ, ānandajāto vipulamalattha pītiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§693.</p>

```
Anekasākhañca sahassamaṇḍalaṃ, chattaṃ marū dhārayumantalikkhe;
```

```
Suvaṇṇadaṇḍā vītipatanti cāmarā, na dissare cāmarachattagāhakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§694.</p>

```
Disvā <pb ed="M" n="0.0387" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0134" /> jaṭī kaṇhasirivhayo isi, suvaṇṇanikkhaṃ viya paṇḍukambale;
```

```
Setañca chattaṃ dhariyanta <note>dhāriyanta (syā.), dhārayantaṃ (sī. ka.)</note> muddhani, udaggacitto sumano paṭiggahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§695.</p>

```
Paṭiggahetvā pana sakyapuṅgavaṃ, jigīsato <note>jigiṃsako (sī. syā. pī.)</note> lakkhaṇamantapāragū;
```

```
Pasannacitto giramabbhudīrayi, ‘‘anuttarāyaṃ dvipadānamuttamo’’ <note>dipadānamuttamo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§696.</p>

```
Athattano gamanamanussaranto, akalyarūpo gaḷayati assukāni;
```

```
Disvāna sakyā isimavocuṃ rudantaṃ,
```

```
‘‘No ce kumāre bhavissati antarāyo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§697.</p>

```
Disvāna sakye isimavoca akalye, ‘‘nāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0469" /> kumāre ahitamanussarāmi;
```

```
Na cāpimassa bhavissati antarāyo, na orakāyaṃ adhimānasā <note>adhimanasā (sī. syā.)</note> bhavātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§698.</p>

```
‘‘Sambodhiyaggaṃ phusissatāyaṃ kumāro, so dhammacakkaṃ paramavisuddhadassī;
```

```
Vattessatāyaṃ bahujanahitānukampī, vitthārikassa bhavissati brahmacariyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§699.</p>

```
‘‘Mamañca <pb ed="P" n="0.0135" /> āyu na ciramidhāvaseso, athantarā me bhavissati kālakiriyā;
```

```
Sohaṃ na sossaṃ <note>sussaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> asamadhurassa dhammaṃ, tenamhi aṭṭo byasanaṃgato aghāvī’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§700.</p>

```
So <pb ed="M" n="0.0388" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0187" /> sākiyānaṃ vipulaṃ janetvā pītiṃ, antepuramhā niggamā <note>niragamā (sī. syā.), nigamā (ka. sī.), niragama (pī.)</note> brahmacārī;
```

```
So bhāgineyyaṃ sayaṃ anukampamāno, samādapesi asamadhurassa dhamme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§701.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhoti ghosaṃ yada <note>yadi (syā. ka.)</note> parato suṇāsi, sambodhipatto vivarati dhammamaggaṃ;
```

```
Gantvāna tattha samayaṃ paripucchamāno <note>sayaṃ paripucchiyāno (sī. syā.)</note>, carassu tasmiṃ bhagavati brahmacariyaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§702.</p>

```
Tenānusiṭṭho hitamanena tādinā, anāgate <pb ed="T" n="0.0470" /> paramavisuddhadassinā;
```

```
So nālako upacitapuññasañcayo, jinaṃ patikkhaṃ <note>pati + ikkhaṃ = patikkhaṃ</note> parivasi rakkhitindriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§703.</p>

```
Sutvāna ghosaṃ jinavaracakkavattane, gantvāna disvā isinisabhaṃ pasanno;
```

```
Moneyyaseṭṭhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0136" /> munipavaraṃ apucchi, samāgate asitāvhayassa sāsaneti.
```

Vatthugāthā niṭṭhitā.

<p rend="hangnum">§704.</p>

```
‘‘Aññātametaṃ vacanaṃ, asitassa yathātathaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ taṃ gotama pucchāmi, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§705.</p>

```
‘‘Anagāriyupetassa, bhikkhācariyaṃ jigīsato;
```

```
Muni pabrūhi me puṭṭho, moneyyaṃ uttamaṃ padaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§706.</p>

```
‘‘Moneyyaṃ te upaññissaṃ, (iti bhagavā) dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃ;
```

```
Handa te naṃ pavakkhāmi, santhambhassu daḷho bhava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§707.</p>

```
‘‘Samānabhāgaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0389" /> kubbetha, gāme akkuṭṭhavanditaṃ;
```

```
Manopadosaṃ rakkheyya, santo anuṇṇato care.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§708.</p>

```
‘‘Uccāvacā <pb ed="V" n="0.0188" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0137" /> niccharanti, dāye aggisikhūpamā;
```

```
Nāriyo muniṃ palobhenti, tāsu taṃ mā palobhayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§709.</p>

```
‘‘Virato methunā dhammā, hitvā kāme paropare <note>parovare (sī. pī.), varāvare (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Aviruddho <pb ed="T" n="0.0471" /> asāratto, pāṇesu tasathāvare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§710.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā ahaṃ tathā ete, yathā ete tathā ahaṃ;
```

```
Attānaṃ upamaṃ katvā, na haneyya na ghātaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§711.</p>

```
‘‘Hitvā icchañca lobhañca, yattha satto puthujjano;
```

```
Cakkhumā paṭipajjeyya, tareyya narakaṃ imaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§712.</p>

```
‘‘Ūnūdaro mitāhāro, appicchassa alolupo;
```

```
Sadā <note>sa ve (pī.)</note> icchāya nicchāto, aniccho hoti nibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§713.</p>

```
‘‘Sa piṇḍacāraṃ caritvā, vanantamabhihāraye;
```

```
Upaṭṭhito rukkhamūlasmiṃ, āsanūpagato muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§714.</p>

```
‘‘Sa jhānapasuto dhīro, vanante ramito siyā;
```

```
Jhāyetha rukkhamūlasmiṃ, attānamabhitosayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§715.</p>

```
‘‘Tato ratyā vivasāne <note>vivasane (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, gāmantamabhihāraye;
```

```
Avhānaṃ nābhinandeyya, abhihārañca gāmato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§716.</p>

```
‘‘Na munī gāmamāgamma, kulesu sahasā care;
```

```
Ghāsesanaṃ chinnakatho, na vācaṃ payutaṃ bhaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§717.</p>

```
‘‘Alatthaṃ yadidaṃ sādhu, nālatthaṃ kusalaṃ iti;
```

```
Ubhayeneva so tādī, rukkhaṃvupanivattati <note>rukkhaṃvu’pativattati (ka.), rukkhaṃva upātivattati (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§718.</p>

```
‘‘Sa <pb ed="V" n="0.0189" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0138" /> pattapāṇi vicaranto, amūgo mūgasammato;
```

```
Appaṃ dānaṃ na hīḷeyya, dātāraṃ nāvajāniyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§719.</p>

```
‘‘Uccāvacā <pb ed="M" n="0.0390" /> hi paṭipadā, samaṇena pakāsitā;
```

```
Na pāraṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0472" /> diguṇaṃ yanti, nayidaṃ ekaguṇaṃ mutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§720.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa ca visatā natthi, chinnasotassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Kiccākiccappahīnassa, pariḷāho na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§721.</p>

```
‘‘Moneyyaṃ te upaññissaṃ, khuradhārūpamo bhave;
```

```
Jivhāya tālumāhacca, udare saññato siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§722.</p>

```
‘‘Alīnacitto ca siyā, na cāpi bahu cintaye;
```

```
Nirāmagandho asito, brahmacariyaparāyaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§723.</p>

```
‘‘Ekāsanassa sikkhetha, samaṇūpāsanassa ca;
```

```
Ekattaṃ monamakkhātaṃ, eko ce abhiramissasi;
```

```
Atha bhāhisi <note>bhāsihi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dasadisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§724.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā dhīrānaṃ nigghosaṃ, jhāyīnaṃ kāmacāginaṃ;
```

```
Tato hiriñca saddhañca, bhiyyo kubbetha māmako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§725.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0139" /> nadīhi vijānātha, sobbhesu padaresu ca;
```

```
Saṇantā yanti kusobbhā <note>kussubbhā (sī.)</note>, tuṇhīyanti mahodadhī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§726.</p>

```
‘‘Yadūnakaṃ taṃ saṇati, yaṃ pūraṃ santameva taṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhakumbhūpamo bālo, rahado pūrova paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§727.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ samaṇo bahuṃ bhāsati, upetaṃ atthasañhitaṃ;
```

```
Jānaṃ so dhammaṃ deseti, jānaṃ so bahu bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§728.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="0.0190" /> ca jānaṃ saṃyatatto, jānaṃ na bahu bhāsati;
```

```
Sa <pb ed="T" n="0.0473" /> munī monamarahati, sa munī monamajjhagā’’ti.
```

Nālakasuttaṃ ekādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 12. Dvayatānupassanāsuttaṃ

Evaṃ me sutaṃ – ekaṃ samayaṃ bhagavā sāvatthiyaṃ viharati pubbārāme migāramātupāsāde. Tena kho pana samayena bhagavā tadahuposathe pannarase <pb ed="M" n="0.0391" /> puṇṇāya puṇṇamāya rattiyā bhikkhusaṅghaparivuto abbhokāse nisinno hoti<pb ed="P" n="0.0140" />. Atha kho bhagavā tuṇhībhūtaṃ tuṇhībhūtaṃ bhikkhusaṅghaṃ anuviloketvā bhikkhū āmantesi –

‘‘‘Ye te, bhikkhave, kusalā dhammā ariyā niyyānikā sambodhagāmino, tesaṃ vo, bhikkhave, kusalānaṃ dhammānaṃ ariyānaṃ niyyānikānaṃ sambodhagāmīnaṃ kā upanisā savanāyā’ti iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu, te evamassu vacanīyā – ‘yāvadeva dvayatānaṃ dhammānaṃ yathābhūtaṃ ñāṇāyā’ti. Kiñca dvayataṃ vadetha?

(1) ‘‘Idaṃ dukkhaṃ, ayaṃ dukkhasamudayoti ayamekānupassanā. Ayaṃ dukkhanirodho, ayaṃ dukkhanirodhagāminī paṭipadāti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā dvayatānupassino kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato dvinnaṃ phalānaṃ aññataraṃ phalaṃ pāṭikaṅkhaṃ – diṭṭheva dhamme aññā, sati vā <pb ed="T" n="0.0474" /> upādisese anāgāmitā’’ti.

Idamavoca bhagavā. Idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§729.</p>

```
‘‘Ye dukkhaṃ nappajānanti, atho dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaṃ, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
```

```
Tañca maggaṃ na jānanti, dukkhūpasamagāminaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§730.</p>

```
‘‘Cetovimuttihīnā te, atho paññāvimuttiyā;
```

```
Abhabbā te antakiriyāya, te ve jātijarūpagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§731.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="V" n="0.0191" /> ca dukkhaṃ pajānanti, atho dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Yattha ca sabbaso dukkhaṃ, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
```

```
Tañca <pb ed="P" n="0.0141" /> maggaṃ pajānanti, dukkhūpasamagāminaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§732.</p>

```
‘‘Cetovimuttisampannā, atho paññāvimuttiyā;
```

```
Bhabbā te antakiriyāya, na te jātijarūpagā’’ti.
```

(2) ‘‘‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. Kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ upadhipaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Upadhīnaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0392" /> tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§733.</p>

```
‘‘Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā, ye <pb ed="T" n="0.0475" /> keci lokasmimanekarūpā;
```

```
Yo ve avidvā upadhiṃ karoti, punappunaṃ dukkhamupeti mando;
```

```
Tasmā pajānaṃ upadhiṃ na kayirā, dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassī’’ti.
```

(3) ‘‘‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. Kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ avijjāpaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Avijjāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§734.</p>

```
‘‘Jātimaraṇasaṃsāraṃ<pb ed="P" n="0.0142" />, ye vajanti punappunaṃ;
```

```
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, avijjāyeva sā gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§735.</p>

```
‘‘Avijjā hāyaṃ mahāmoho, yenidaṃ saṃsitaṃ ciraṃ;
```

```
Vijjāgatā ca ye sattā, na te gacchanti <note>nāgacchanti (sī. pī.)</note> punabbhava’’nti.
```

(4) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ saṅkhārapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Saṅkhārānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§736.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0192" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0476" /> kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ saṅkhārapaccayā;
```

```
Saṅkhārānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§737.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ saṅkhārapaccayā;
```

```
Sabbasaṅkhārasamathā, saññānaṃ uparodhanā;
```

```
Evaṃ dukkhakkhayo hoti, etaṃ ñatvā yathātathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§738.</p>

```
‘‘Sammaddasā vedaguno, sammadaññāya paṇḍitā;
```

```
Abhibhuyya mārasaṃyogaṃ, na gacchanti <note>nāgacchanti (sī. pī.)</note> punabbhava’’nti.
```

(5) ‘‘Siyā <pb ed="M" n="0.0393" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0143" /> aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ viññāṇapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Viññāṇassa tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§739.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ viññāṇapaccayā;
```

```
Viññāṇassa nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§740.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ viññāṇapaccayā;
```

```
Viññāṇūpasamā bhikkhu, nicchāto parinibbuto’’ti.
```

(6) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ phassapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Phassassa tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca <pb ed="T" n="0.0477" /> satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§741.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ phassaparetānaṃ, bhavasotānusārinaṃ;
```

```
Kummaggapaṭipannānaṃ, ārā saṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§742.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca phassaṃ pariññāya, aññāyupasame <note>paññāya upasame (syā.)</note> ratā;
```

```
Te ve phassābhisamayā, nicchātā parinibbutā’’ti.
```

(7) ‘‘Siyā <pb ed="V" n="0.0193" /> aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ vedanāpaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Vedanānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§743.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0144" /> vā yadi vā dukkhaṃ, adukkhamasukhaṃ saha;
```

```
Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, yaṃ kiñci atthi veditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§744.</p>

```
‘‘Etaṃ dukkhanti ñatvāna, mosadhammaṃ palokinaṃ <note>palokitaṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Phussa phussa vayaṃ passaṃ, evaṃ tattha vijānati <note>virajjati (ka. sī.)</note>;
```

```
Vedanānaṃ khayā bhikkhu, nicchāto parinibbuto’’ti.
```

(8) ‘‘Siyā <pb ed="M" n="0.0394" /> aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ taṇhāpaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Taṇhāya tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§745.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhādutiyo <pb ed="T" n="0.0478" /> puriso, dīghamaddhāna saṃsaraṃ;
```

```
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, saṃsāraṃ nātivattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§746.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, taṇhaṃ <note>taṇhā (bahūsu) itivuttake 15 passitabbaṃ</note> dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Vītataṇho anādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

(9) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ upādānapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Upādānānaṃ <note>upādānassa (syā. ka.)</note> tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§747.</p>

```
‘‘Upādānapaccayā bhavo, bhūto dukkhaṃ nigacchati;
```

```
Jātassa maraṇaṃ hoti, eso dukkhassa sambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§748.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā upādānakkhayā, sammadaññāya paṇḍitā;
```

```
Jātikkhayaṃ abhiññāya, na gacchanti punabbhava’’nti.
```

(10) ‘‘Siyā <pb ed="V" n="0.0194" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0145" /> aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ ārambhapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Ārambhānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§749.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ ārambhapaccayā;
```

```
Ārambhānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§750.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0479" /> ñatvā, dukkhaṃ ārambhapaccayā;
```

```
Sabbārambhaṃ paṭinissajja, anārambhe vimuttino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§751.</p>

```
‘‘Ucchinnabhavataṇhassa, santacittassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Vikkhīṇo <note>vitiṇṇo (sī.)</note> jātisaṃsāro, natthi tassa punabbhavo’’ti.
```

(11) ‘‘Siyā <pb ed="M" n="0.0395" /> aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ āhārapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Āhārānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§752.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ āhārapaccayā;
```

```
Āhārānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§753.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ āhārapaccayā;
```

```
Sabbāhāraṃ pariññāya, sabbāhāramanissito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§754.</p>

```
‘‘Ārogyaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0146" /> sammadaññāya, āsavānaṃ parikkhayā;
```

```
Saṅkhāya sevī dhammaṭṭho, saṅkhyaṃ <note>saṅkhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> nopeti vedagū’’ti.
```

(12) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti sabbaṃ iñjitapaccayāti, ayamekānupassanā. Iñjitānaṃ tveva asesavirāganirodhā natthi dukkhassa sambhavoti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§755.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0195" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0480" /> kiñci dukkhaṃ sambhoti, sabbaṃ iñjitapaccayā;
```

```
Iñjitānaṃ nirodhena, natthi dukkhassa sambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§756.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, dukkhaṃ iñjitapaccayā;
```

```
Tasmā hi ejaṃ vossajja, saṅkhāre uparundhiya;
```

```
Anejo anupādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

(13) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Nissitassa calitaṃ hotīti, ayamekānupassanā. Anissito na calatīti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§757.</p>

```
‘‘Anissito na calati, nissito ca upādiyaṃ;
```

```
Itthabhāvaññathābhāvaṃ, saṃsāraṃ nātivattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§758.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ ñatvā, nissayesu mahabbhayaṃ;
```

```
Anissito anupādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

(14) ‘‘Siyā <pb ed="M" n="0.0396" /> aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Rūpehi, bhikkhave, arūpā <note>āruppā (sī. pī.)</note> santatarāti, ayamekānupassanā. Arūpehi <pb ed="P" n="0.0147" /> nirodho santataroti, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§759.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca rūpūpagā sattā, ye ca arūpaṭṭhāyino <note>āruppavāsino (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nirodhaṃ appajānantā, āgantāro punabbhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§760.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca rūpe pariññāya, arūpesu asaṇṭhitā <note>susaṇṭhitā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nirodhe <pb ed="T" n="0.0481" /> ye vimuccanti, te janā maccuhāyino’’ti.
```

(15) ‘‘Siyā aññenapi…pe… kathañca siyā? Yaṃ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa lokassa samārakassa sabrahmakassa sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya idaṃ saccanti upanijjhāyitaṃ tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ musāti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayamekānupassanā. Yaṃ<pb ed="V" n="0.0196" />, bhikkhave, sadevakassa…pe… sadevamanussāya idaṃ musāti upanijjhāyitaṃ, tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ saccanti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayaṃ dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā…pe… athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§761.</p>

```
‘‘Anattani attamāniṃ <note>attamānī (syā.), attamānaṃ (pī. ka.)</note>, passa lokaṃ sadevakaṃ;
```

```
Niviṭṭhaṃ nāmarūpasmiṃ, idaṃ saccanti maññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§762.</p>

```
‘‘Yena yena hi maññanti, tato taṃ hoti aññathā;
```

```
Tañhi tassa musā hoti, mosadhammañhi ittaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§763.</p>

```
‘‘Amosadhammaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0148" /> nibbānaṃ, tadariyā saccato vidū;
```

```
Te ve saccābhisamayā, nicchātā parinibbutā’’ti.
```

(16) ‘‘‘Siyā aññenapi pariyāyena sammā dvayatānupassanā’ti, iti ce, bhikkhave, pucchitāro assu; ‘siyā’tissu vacanīyā. Kathañca siyā? Yaṃ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa lokassa samārakassa sabrahmakassa sassamaṇabrāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya idaṃ sukhanti upanijjhāyitaṃ, tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ dukkhanti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayamekānupassanā<pb ed="T" n="0.0482" />. Yaṃ, bhikkhave, sadevakassa…pe… sadevamanussāya idaṃ dukkhanti upanijjhāyitaṃ tadamariyānaṃ etaṃ sukhanti yathābhūtaṃ sammappaññāya sudiṭṭhaṃ, ayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0397" /> dutiyānupassanā. Evaṃ sammā dvayatānupassino kho, bhikkhave, bhikkhuno appamattassa ātāpino pahitattassa viharato dvinnaṃ phalānaṃ aññataraṃ phalaṃ pāṭikaṅkhaṃ – diṭṭheva dhamme aññā, sati vā upādisese anāgāmitāti. Idamavoca bhagavā. Idaṃ vatvāna sugato athāparaṃ etadavoca satthā –

<p rend="hangnum">§764.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpā saddā rasā gandhā, phassā dhammā ca kevalā;
```

```
Iṭṭhā kantā manāpā ca, yāvatatthīti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§765.</p>

```
‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, ete vo sukhasammatā;
```

```
Yattha cete nirujjhanti, taṃ nesaṃ dukkhasammataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§766.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhanti <pb ed="V" n="0.0197" /> diṭṭhamariyehi, sakkāyassuparodhanaṃ;
```

```
Paccanīkamidaṃ hoti, sabbalokena passataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§767.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0149" /> pare sukhato āhu, tadariyā āhu dukkhato;
```

```
Yaṃ pare dukkhato āhu, tadariyā sukhato vidū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§768.</p>

```
‘‘Passa dhammaṃ durājānaṃ, sampamūḷhetthaviddasu <note>sampamūḷhettha aviddasu (sī. pī.), sammūḷhettha aviddasu (?)</note>;
```

```
Nivutānaṃ tamo hoti, andhakāro apassataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§769.</p>

```
‘‘Satañca vivaṭaṃ hoti, āloko passatāmiva;
```

```
Santike na vijānanti, maggā dhammassa kovidā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§770.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavarāgaparetehi<pb ed="T" n="0.0483" />, bhavasotānusāribhi;
```

```
Māradheyyānupannehi, nāyaṃ dhammo susambudho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§771.</p>

```
‘‘Ko nu aññatramariyehi, padaṃ sambuddhumarahati;
```

```
Yaṃ padaṃ sammadaññāya, parinibbanti anāsavā’’ti.
```

Idamavoca bhagavā. Attamanā te bhikkhū bhagavato bhāsitaṃ abhinandunti. Imasmiṃ ca <note>imasmiṃ kho (sī.)</note> pana veyyākaraṇasmiṃ bhaññamāne saṭṭhimattānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ anupādāya āsavehi cittāni vimucciṃsūti.

Dvayatānupassanāsuttaṃ dvādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0150" /> –

```
Saccaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0398" /> upadhi avijjā ca, saṅkhāre viññāṇapañcamaṃ;
```

```
Phassavedaniyā taṇhā, upādānārambhaāhārā;
```

```
Iñjitaṃ calitaṃ rūpaṃ, saccaṃ dukkhena soḷasāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Mahāvaggo tatiyo niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0198" /> –

```
Pabbajjā ca padhānañca, subhāsitañca sundari;
```

```
Māghasuttaṃ sabhiyo ca, selo sallañca vuccati.
```

```
Vāseṭṭho cāpi kokāli, nālako dvayatānupassanā;
```

```
Dvādasetāni suttāni, mahāvaggoti vuccatīti.
```

### 4. Aṭṭhakavaggo

#### 1. Kāmasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§772.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0399" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0199" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0151" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0484" /> kāmayamānassa, tassa ce taṃ samijjhati;
```

```
Addhā pītimano hoti, laddhā macco yadicchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§773.</p>

```
Tassa ce kāmayānassa <note>kāmayamānassa (ka.)</note>, chandajātassa jantuno;
```

```
Te kāmā parihāyanti, sallaviddhova ruppati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§774.</p>

```
Yo kāme parivajjeti, sappasseva padā siro;
```

```
Somaṃ <note>so imaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> visattikaṃ loke, sato samativattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§775.</p>

```
Khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraññaṃ vā, gavassaṃ <note>gavāssaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dāsaporisaṃ;
```

```
Thiyo bandhū puthu kāme, yo naro anugijjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§776.</p>

```
Abalā naṃ balīyanti, maddantenaṃ parissayā;
```

```
Tato naṃ dukkhamanveti, nāvaṃ bhinnamivodakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§777.</p>

```
Tasmā jantu sadā sato, kāmāni parivajjaye;
```

```
Te pahāya tare oghaṃ, nāvaṃ sitvāva <note>siñcitvā (sī.)</note> pāragūti.
```

Kāmasuttaṃ paṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 2. Guhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§778.</p>

```
Satto <pb ed="V" n="0.0200" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0485" /> guhāyaṃ bahunābhichanno, tiṭṭhaṃ naro mohanasmiṃ pagāḷho;
```

```
Dūre <pb ed="P" n="0.0152" /> vivekā hi tathāvidho so, kāmā hi loke na hi suppahāyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§779.</p>

```
Icchānidānā <pb ed="M" n="0.0400" /> bhavasātabaddhā, te duppamuñcā na hi aññamokkhā;
```

```
Pacchā pure vāpi apekkhamānā, imeva kāme purimeva jappaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§780.</p>

```
Kāmesu giddhā pasutā pamūḷhā, avadāniyā te visame niviṭṭhā;
```

```
Dukkhūpanītā paridevayanti, kiṃsū bhavissāma ito cutāse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§781.</p>

```
Tasmā hi sikkhetha idheva jantu, yaṃ kiñci jaññā visamanti loke;
```

```
Na tassa hetū visamaṃ careyya, appañhidaṃ jīvitamāhu dhīrā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§782.</p>

```
Passāmi loke pariphandamānaṃ, pajaṃ imaṃ taṇhagataṃ bhavesu;
```

```
Hīnā <pb ed="T" n="0.0486" /> narā maccumukhe lapanti, avītataṇhāse bhavābhavesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§783.</p>

```
Mamāyite passatha phandamāne, maccheva appodake khīṇasote;
```

```
Etampi disvā amamo careyya, bhavesu āsattimakubbamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§784.</p>

```
Ubhosu antesu vineyya chandaṃ, phassaṃ pariññāya anānugiddho;
```

```
Yadattagarahī tadakubbamāno, na lippatī <note>na limpatī (syā. ka.)</note> diṭṭhasutesu dhīro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§785.</p>

```
Saññaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0153" /> pariññā vitareyya oghaṃ, pariggahesu muni nopalitto;
```

```
Abbūḷhasallo caramappamatto, nāsīsatī <note>nāsiṃsatī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> lokamimaṃ parañcāti.
```

Guhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ dutiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 3. Duṭṭhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§786.</p>

```
Vadanti <pb ed="M" n="0.0401" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0201" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0487" /> ve duṭṭhamanāpi eke, athopi ve saccamanā vadanti;
```

```
Vādañca jātaṃ muni no upeti, tasmā munī natthi khilo kuhiñci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§787.</p>

```
Sakañhi diṭṭhiṃ kathamaccayeyya, chandānunīto ruciyā niviṭṭho;
```

```
Sayaṃ samattāni pakubbamāno, yathā hi jāneyya tathā vadeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§788.</p>

```
Yo attano sīlavatāni jantu, anānupuṭṭhova paresa <note>parassa (ka.)</note> pāva <note>pāvā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Anariyadhammaṃ kusalā tamāhu, yo ātumānaṃ sayameva pāva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§789.</p>

```
Santo ca bhikkhu abhinibbutatto, itihanti sīlesu akatthamāno;
```

```
Tamariyadhammaṃ kusalā vadanti, yassussadā natthi kuhiñci loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§790.</p>

```
Pakappitā <pb ed="P" n="0.0154" /> saṅkhatā yassa dhammā, purakkhatā <note>purekkhatā (sī.)</note> santi avīvadātā;
```

```
Yadattani <pb ed="T" n="0.0488" /> passati ānisaṃsaṃ, taṃ nissito kuppapaṭicca santiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§791.</p>

```
Diṭṭhīnivesā na hi svātivattā, dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā naro tesu nivesanesu, nirassatī ādiyatī ca dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§792.</p>

```
Dhonassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0402" /> hi natthi kuhiñci loke, pakappitā diṭṭhi bhavābhavesu;
```

```
Māyañca mānañca pahāya dhono, sa kena gaccheyya anūpayo so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§793.</p>

```
Upayo hi dhammesu upeti vādaṃ, anūpayaṃ kena kathaṃ vadeyya;
```

```
Attā nirattā <note>attaṃ nirattaṃ (bahūsu)</note> na hi tassa atthi, adhosi so diṭṭhimidheva sabbanti.
```

Duṭṭhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ tatiyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 4. Suddhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§794.</p>

```
Passāmi <pb ed="V" n="0.0202" /> suddhaṃ paramaṃ arogaṃ, diṭṭhena saṃsuddhi narassa hoti;
```

```
Evābhijānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0489" /> <note>etābhijānaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> paramanti ñatvā, suddhānupassīti pacceti ñāṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§795.</p>

```
Diṭṭhena <pb ed="P" n="0.0155" /> ce suddhi narassa hoti, ñāṇena vā so pajahāti dukkhaṃ;
```

```
Aññena so sujjhati sopadhīko, diṭṭhī hi naṃ pāva tathā vadānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§796.</p>

```
Na brāhmaṇo aññato suddhimāha, diṭṭhe sute sīlavate mute vā;
```

```
Puññe ca pāpe ca anūpalitto, attañjaho nayidha pakubbamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§797.</p>

```
Purimaṃ pahāya aparaṃ sitāse, ejānugā te na taranti saṅgaṃ;
```

```
Te uggahāyanti nirassajanti, kapīva sākhaṃ pamuñcaṃ gahāyaṃ <note>pamukhaṃ gahāya (syā.), pamuñca gahāya (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§798.</p>

```
Sayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0403" /> samādāya vatāni jantu, uccāvacaṃ gacchati saññasatto;
```

```
Vidvā ca vedehi samecca dhammaṃ, na uccāvacaṃ gacchati bhūripañño.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§799.</p>

```
Sa sabbadhammesu visenibhūto, yaṃ kiñci diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
```

```
Tameva <pb ed="T" n="0.0490" /> dassiṃ vivaṭaṃ carantaṃ, kenīdha lokasmi vikappayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§800.</p>

```
Na kappayanti na purekkharonti, accantasuddhīti na te vadanti;
```

```
Ādānaganthaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0156" /> gathitaṃ visajja, āsaṃ na kubbanti kuhiñci loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§801.</p>

```
Sīmātigo brāhmaṇo tassa natthi, ñatvā va disvā va <note>ñatvā ca disvā ca (ka. sī. ka.)</note> samuggahītaṃ;
```

```
Na rāgarāgī na virāgaratto, tassīdha natthī paramuggahītanti.
```

Suddhaṭṭhakasuttaṃ catutthaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 5. Paramaṭṭhakasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§802.</p>

```
Paramanti <pb ed="V" n="0.0203" /> diṭṭhīsu paribbasāno, yaduttari kurute jantu loke;
```

```
Hīnāti aññe tato sabbamāha, tasmā vivādāni avītivatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§803.</p>

```
Yadattanī passati ānisaṃsaṃ, diṭṭhe <pb ed="T" n="0.0491" /> sute sīlavate <note>sīlabbate (syā.)</note> mute vā;
```

```
Tadeva so tattha samuggahāya, nihīnato passati sabbamaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§804.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0404" /> vāpi ganthaṃ kusalā vadanti, yaṃ nissito passati hīnamaññaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā hi diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā, sīlabbataṃ bhikkhu na nissayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§805.</p>

```
Diṭṭhimpi <pb ed="P" n="0.0157" /> lokasmiṃ na kappayeyya, ñāṇena vā sīlavatena vāpi;
```

```
Samoti attānamanūpaneyya, hīno na maññetha visesi vāpi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§806.</p>

```
Attaṃ pahāya anupādiyāno, ñāṇepi so nissayaṃ no karoti;
```

```
Sa ve viyattesu <note>viyuttesu (sī. aṭṭha.), dviyattesu (ka.)</note> na vaggasārī, diṭṭhimpi <note>diṭṭhimapi (ka.)</note> so na pacceti kiñci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§807.</p>

```
Yassūbhayante paṇidhīdha natthi, bhavābhavāya idha vā huraṃ vā;
```

```
Nivesanā tassa na santi keci, dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§808.</p>

```
Tassīdha diṭṭhe va sute mute vā, pakappitā <pb ed="T" n="0.0492" /> natthi aṇūpi saññā;
```

```
Taṃ brāhmaṇaṃ diṭṭhimanādiyānaṃ, kenīdha lokasmiṃ vikappayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§809.</p>

```
Na kappayanti na purekkharonti, dhammāpi tesaṃ na paṭicchitāse;
```

```
Na <pb ed="P" n="0.0158" /> brāhmaṇo sīlavatena neyyo, pāraṅgato na pacceti tādīti.
```

Paramaṭṭhakasuttaṃ pañcamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 6. Jarāsuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§810.</p>

```
Appaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0405" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0204" /> vata jīvitaṃ idaṃ, oraṃ vassasatāpi miyyati <note>mīyati (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Yo cepi aticca jīvati, atha kho so jarasāpi miyyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§811.</p>

```
Socanti janā mamāyite, na hi santi <note>na hi santā (sī.), na hī santi (katthaci)</note> niccā pariggahā;
```

```
Vinābhāvasantamevidaṃ, iti disvā nāgāramāvase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§812.</p>

```
Maraṇenapi taṃ pahīyati <note>pahiyyati (sī. syā. ka.)</note>, yaṃ puriso mamidanti <note>mamayidanti (sī. syā. ka.), mamāyanti (ka.)</note> maññati;
```

```
Etampi viditvā <note>etaṃ disvāna (niddese), etampi viditva (?)</note> paṇḍito, na mamattāya nametha māmako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§813.</p>

```
Supinena yathāpi saṅgataṃ, paṭibuddho puriso na passati;
```

```
Evampi <pb ed="P" n="0.0159" /> piyāyitaṃ janaṃ, petaṃ kālakataṃ na passati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§814.</p>

```
Diṭṭhāpi <pb ed="T" n="0.0493" /> sutāpi te janā, yesaṃ nāmamidaṃ pavuccati <note>nāmamevā vasissati (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nāmaṃyevāvasissati, akkheyyaṃ petassa jantuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§815.</p>

```
Sokapparidevamaccharaṃ <note>sokaparidevamaccharaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), sokaṃ paridevamaccharaṃ (?)</note>, na jahanti giddhā mamāyite;
```

```
Tasmā munayo pariggahaṃ, hitvā acariṃsu khemadassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§816.</p>

```
Patilīnacarassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0406" /> bhikkhuno, bhajamānassa vivittamāsanaṃ;
```

```
Sāmaggiyamāhu tassa taṃ, yo attānaṃ bhavane na dassaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§817.</p>

```
Sabbattha munī anissito, na piyaṃ kubbati nopi appiyaṃ;
```

```
Tasmiṃ paridevamaccharaṃ, paṇṇe vāri yathā na limpati <note>lippati (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§818.</p>

```
Udabindu yathāpi pokkhare, padume vāri yathā na limpati;
```

```
Evaṃ muni nopalimpati, yadidaṃ diṭṭhasutaṃ mutesu vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§819.</p>

```
Dhono <pb ed="V" n="0.0205" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0160" /> na hi tena maññati, yadidaṃ diṭṭhasutaṃ mutesu vā;
```

```
Nāññena visuddhimicchati, na hi so rajjati no virajjatīti.
```

Jarāsuttaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 7. Tissametteyyasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§820.</p>

```
‘‘Methunamanuyuttassa, (iccāyasmā tisso metteyyo) vighātaṃ brūhi mārisa;
```

```
Sutvāna tava sāsanaṃ, viveke sikkhissāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§821.</p>

```
‘‘Methunamanuyuttassa, (metteyyāti bhagavā) mussate vāpi sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Micchā <pb ed="T" n="0.0494" /> ca paṭipajjati, etaṃ tasmiṃ anāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§822.</p>

```
‘‘Eko <pb ed="M" n="0.0407" /> pubbe caritvāna, methunaṃ yo nisevati;
```

```
Yānaṃ bhantaṃ va taṃ loke, hīnamāhu puthujjanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§823.</p>

```
‘‘Yaso kitti ca yā pubbe, hāyate vāpi tassa sā;
```

```
Etampi disvā sikkhetha, methunaṃ vippahātave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§824.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkappehi pareto so, kapaṇo viya jhāyati;
```

```
Sutvā paresaṃ nigghosaṃ, maṅku hoti tathāvidho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§825.</p>

```
‘‘Atha satthāni kurute, paravādehi codito;
```

```
Esa khvassa mahāgedho, mosavajjaṃ pagāhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§826.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇḍitoti samaññāto, ekacariyaṃ adhiṭṭhito;
```

```
Athāpi <note>sa cāpi (niddese)</note> methune yutto, mandova parikissati <note>parikilissati (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§827.</p>

```
‘‘Etamādīnavaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0206" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0161" /> ñatvā, muni pubbāpare idha;
```

```
Ekacariyaṃ daḷhaṃ kayirā, na nisevetha methunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§828.</p>

```
‘‘Vivekaññeva sikkhetha, etadariyānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Na tena seṭṭho maññetha, sa ve nibbānasantike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§829.</p>

```
‘‘Rittassa munino carato, kāmesu anapekkhino;
```

```
Oghatiṇṇassa pihayanti, kāmesu gadhitā <note>gathitā (sī.)</note> pajā’’ti.
```

Tissametteyyasuttaṃ sattamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 8. Pasūrasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§830.</p>

```
Idheva <pb ed="T" n="0.0495" /> suddhi iti vādayanti <note>vidiyanti (sī. pī.)</note>, nāññesu dhammesu visuddhimāhu;
```

```
Yaṃ nissitā tattha subhaṃ vadānā, paccekasaccesu puthū niviṭṭhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§831.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="M" n="0.0408" /> vādakāmā parisaṃ vigayha, bālaṃ dahantī mithu aññamaññaṃ;
```

```
Vadanti te aññasitā kathojjaṃ, pasaṃsakāmā kusalā vadānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§832.</p>

```
Yutto kathāyaṃ parisāya majjhe, pasaṃsamicchaṃ vinighāti hoti;
```

```
Apāhatasmiṃ pana maṅku hoti, nindāya so kuppati randhamesī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§833.</p>

```
Yamassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0162" /> vādaṃ parihīnamāhu, apāhataṃ pañhavimaṃsakāse;
```

```
Paridevati socati hīnavādo, upaccagā manti anutthunāti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§834.</p>

```
Ete vivādā samaṇesu jātā, etesu ugghāti nighāti hoti;
```

```
Etampi <pb ed="T" n="0.0496" /> disvā virame kathojjaṃ, na haññadatthatthipasaṃsalābhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§835.</p>

```
Pasaṃsito <pb ed="V" n="0.0207" /> vā pana tattha hoti, akkhāya vādaṃ parisāya majjhe;
```

```
So hassatī uṇṇamatī <note>unnamatī (?)</note> ca tena, pappuyya tamatthaṃ yathā mano ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§836.</p>

```
Yā uṇṇatī <note>unnatī (?)</note> sāssa vighātabhūmi, mānātimānaṃ vadate paneso;
```

```
Etampi disvā na vivādayetha, na hi tena suddhiṃ kusalā vadanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§837.</p>

```
Sūro yathā rājakhādāya puṭṭho, abhigajjameti paṭisūramicchaṃ;
```

```
Yeneva so tena palehi sūra, pubbeva natthi yadidaṃ yudhāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§838.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="M" n="0.0409" /> diṭṭhimuggayha vivādayanti <note>vivādiyanti (sī. pī.)</note>, idameva saccanti ca vādayanti;
```

```
Te <pb ed="P" n="0.0163" /> tvaṃ vadassū na hi tedha atthi, vādamhi jāte paṭisenikattā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§839.</p>

```
Visenikatvā pana ye caranti, diṭṭhīhi diṭṭhiṃ avirujjhamānā;
```

```
Tesu <pb ed="T" n="0.0497" /> tvaṃ kiṃ labhetho pasūra, yesīdha natthī paramuggahītaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§840.</p>

```
Atha tvaṃ pavitakkamāgamā, manasā diṭṭhigatāni cintayanto;
```

```
Dhonena yugaṃ samāgamā, na hi tvaṃ sakkhasi sampayātaveti.
```

Pasūrasuttaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 9. Māgaṇḍiyasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§841.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna taṇhaṃ aratiṃ ragañca <note>aratiñca rāgaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>, nāhosi chando api methunasmiṃ;
```

```
Kimevidaṃ muttakarīsapuṇṇaṃ, pādāpi naṃ samphusituṃ na icche’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§842.</p>

```
‘‘Etādisaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0164" /> ce ratanaṃ na icchasi, nāriṃ narindehi bahūhi patthitaṃ;
```

```
Diṭṭhigataṃ sīlavataṃ nu jīvitaṃ <note>sīlavatānujīvitaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, bhavūpapattiñca vadesi kīdisaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§843.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0208" /> vadāmīti na tassa hoti, (māgaṇḍiyāti <note>māgandiyāti (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhagavā)
```

```
Dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ;
```

```
Passañca <pb ed="T" n="0.0498" /> diṭṭhīsu anuggahāya,
```

```
Ajjhattasantiṃ pacinaṃ adassaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§844.</p>

```
‘‘Vinicchayā <pb ed="M" n="0.0410" /> yāni pakappitāni, (iti māgaṇḍiyo <note>māgandiyo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> )
```

```
Te ve munī brūsi anuggahāya;
```

```
Ajjhattasantīti yametamatthaṃ,
```

```
Kathaṃ nu dhīrehi paveditaṃ taṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§845.</p>

```
‘‘Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā)
```

```
Sīlabbatenāpi na suddhimāha;
```

```
Adiṭṭhiyā assutiyā añāṇā,
```

```
Asīlatā abbatā nopi tena;
```

```
Ete ca nissajja anuggahāya,
```

```
Santo anissāya bhavaṃ na jappe’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§846.</p>

```
‘‘No ce kira diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (iti māgaṇḍiyo)
```

```
Sīlabbatenāpi na suddhimāha;
```

```
Adiṭṭhiyā <pb ed="P" n="0.0165" /> assutiyā añāṇā,
```

```
Asīlatā abbatā nopi tena;
```

```
Maññāmahaṃ momuhameva dhammaṃ,
```

```
Diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§847.</p>

```
‘‘Diṭṭhañca nissāya anupucchamāno, (māgaṇḍiyāti bhagavā)
```

```
Samuggahītesu pamohamāgā <note>samohamāgā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ito <pb ed="T" n="0.0499" /> ca nāddakkhi aṇumpi saññaṃ,
```

```
Tasmā tuvaṃ momuhato dahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§848.</p>

```
‘‘Samo <pb ed="V" n="0.0209" /> visesī uda vā nihīno, yo maññatī so vivadetha tena;
```

```
Tīsu vidhāsu avikampamāno, samo visesīti na tassa hoti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§849.</p>

```
‘‘Saccanti so brāhmaṇo kiṃ vadeyya, musāti vā so vivadetha kena;
```

```
Yasmiṃ samaṃ visamaṃ vāpi natthi, sa kena vādaṃ paṭisaṃyujeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§850.</p>

```
‘‘Okaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0411" /> pahāya aniketasārī, gāme akubbaṃ muni santhavāni <note>sandhavāni (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Kāmehi ritto apurekkharāno, kathaṃ na viggayha janena kayirā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§851.</p>

```
‘‘Yehi vivitto vicareyya loke, na tāni uggayha vadeyya nāgo;
```

```
Jalambujaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0166" /> <note>elambujaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> kaṇḍakaṃ vārijaṃ yathā, jalena paṅkena canūpalittaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ munī santivādo agiddho, kāme ca loke ca anūpalitto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§852.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="T" n="0.0500" /> vedagū diṭṭhiyāyako <note>na vedagū diṭṭhiyā (ka. sī. syā. pī.)</note> na mutiyā, sa mānameti na hi tammayo so;
```

```
Na kammunā nopi sutena neyyo, anūpanīto sa nivesanesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§853.</p>

```
‘‘Saññāvirattassa na santi ganthā, paññāvimuttassa na santi mohā;
```

```
Saññañca diṭṭhiñca ye aggahesuṃ, te ghaṭṭayantā <note>ghaṭṭamānā (syā. ka.)</note> vicaranti loke’’ti.
```

Māgaṇḍiyasuttaṃ navamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 10. Purābhedasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§854.</p>

```
‘‘Kathaṃdassī kathaṃsīlo, upasantoti vuccati;
```

```
Taṃ me gotama pabrūhi, pucchito uttamaṃ naraṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§855.</p>

```
‘‘Vītataṇho purā bhedā, (iti bhagavā) pubbamantamanissito;
```

```
Vemajjhe nupasaṅkheyyo, tassa natthi purakkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§856.</p>

```
‘‘Akkodhano <pb ed="M" n="0.0412" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0210" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0167" /> asantāsī, avikatthī akukkuco;
```

```
Mantabhāṇī <note>mantābhāṇī (syā. pī.)</note> anuddhato, sa ve vācāyato muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§857.</p>

```
‘‘Nirāsatti anāgate, atītaṃ nānusocati;
```

```
Vivekadassī phassesu, diṭṭhīsu ca na nīyati <note>niyyati (bahūsu)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§858.</p>

```
‘‘Patilīno akuhako, apihālu amaccharī;
```

```
Appagabbho <pb ed="T" n="0.0501" /> ajeguccho, pesuṇeyye ca no yuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§859.</p>

```
‘‘Sātiyesu anassāvī, atimāne ca no yuto;
```

```
Saṇho ca paṭibhānavā <note>paṭibhāṇavā (syā. pī.)</note>, na saddho na virajjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§860.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhakamyā na sikkhati, alābhe ca na kuppati;
```

```
Aviruddho ca taṇhāya, rasesu nānugijjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§861.</p>

```
‘‘Upekkhako sadā sato, na loke maññate samaṃ;
```

```
Na visesī na nīceyyo, tassa no santi ussadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§862.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa nissayanā <note>nissayatā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> natthi, ñatvā dhammaṃ anissito;
```

```
Bhavāya vibhavāya vā, taṇhā yassa na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§863.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ brūmi upasantoti, kāmesu anapekkhinaṃ;
```

```
Ganthā tassa na vijjanti, atarī so visattikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§864.</p>

```
‘‘Na tassa puttā pasavo, khettaṃ vatthuñca vijjati;
```

```
Attā <pb ed="P" n="0.0168" /> vāpi nirattā vā <note>attaṃ vāpi nirattaṃ vā (bahūsu)</note>, na tasmiṃ upalabbhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§865.</p>

```
‘‘Yena naṃ vajjuṃ puthujjanā, atho samaṇabrāhmaṇā;
```

```
Taṃ tassa apurakkhataṃ, tasmā vādesu nejati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§866.</p>

```
‘‘Vītagedho <pb ed="V" n="0.0211" /> amaccharī, na ussesu vadate muni;
```

```
Na samesu na omesu, kappaṃ neti akappiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§867.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa loke sakaṃ natthi, asatā ca na socati;
```

```
Dhammesu ca na gacchati, sa ve santoti vuccatī’’ti.
```

Purābhedasuttaṃ dasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 11. Kalahavivādasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§868.</p>

```
‘‘Kutopahūtā <pb ed="M" n="0.0413" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0502" /> kalahā vivādā, paridevasokā sahamaccharā ca;
```

```
Mānātimānā sahapesuṇā ca, kutopahūtā te tadiṅgha brūhi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§869.</p>

```
‘‘Piyappahūtā kalahā vivādā,
```

```
Paridevasokā sahamaccharā ca;
```

```
Mānātimānā sahapesuṇā ca,
```

```
Maccherayuttā kalahā vivādā;
```

```
Vivādajātesu ca pesuṇāni’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§870.</p>

```
‘‘Piyā <pb ed="P" n="0.0169" /> su <note>piyānu (syā.), piyassu (ka.)</note> lokasmiṃ kutonidānā, ye cāpi <note>ye vāpi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> lobhā vicaranti loke;
```

```
Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca kutonidānā, ye samparāyāya narassa honti’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§871.</p>

```
‘‘Chandānidānāni piyāni loke, ye cāpi lobhā vicaranti loke;
```

```
Āsā ca niṭṭhā ca itonidānā, ye samparāyāya narassa honti’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§872.</p>

```
‘‘Chando <pb ed="T" n="0.0503" /> nu lokasmiṃ kutonidāno, vinicchayā cāpi <note>vāpi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kutopahūtā;
```

```
Kodho mosavajjañca kathaṃkathā ca, ye vāpi dhammā samaṇena vuttā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§873.</p>

```
‘‘Sātaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0212" /> asātanti yamāhu loke, tamūpanissāya pahoti chando;
```

```
Rūpesu disvā vibhavaṃ bhavañca, vinicchayaṃ kubbati <note>kurute (bahūsu)</note> jantu loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§874.</p>

```
‘‘Kodho <pb ed="M" n="0.0414" /> mosavajjañca kathaṃkathā ca, etepi dhammā dvayameva sante;
```

```
Kathaṃkathī ñāṇapathāya sikkhe, ñatvā pavuttā samaṇena dhammā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§875.</p>

```
‘‘Sātaṃ asātañca kutonidānā, kismiṃ asante na bhavanti hete;
```

```
Vibhavaṃ bhavañcāpi yametamatthaṃ, etaṃ me pabrūhi yatonidānaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§876.</p>

```
‘‘Phassanidānaṃ sātaṃ asātaṃ, phasse asante na bhavanti hete;
```

```
Vibhavaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0170" /> bhavañcāpi yametamatthaṃ, etaṃ te pabrūmi itonidānaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§877.</p>

```
‘‘Phasso <pb ed="T" n="0.0504" /> nu lokasmi kutonidāno, pariggahā cāpi kutopahūtā;
```

```
Kismiṃ asante na mamattamatthi, kismiṃ vibhūte na phusanti phassā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§878.</p>

```
‘‘Nāmañca rūpañca paṭicca phasso, icchānidānāni pariggahāni;
```

```
Icchāyasantyā na mamattamatthi, rūpe vibhūte na phusanti phassā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§879.</p>

```
‘‘Kathaṃsametassa vibhoti rūpaṃ, sukhaṃ dukhañcāpi <note>dukhaṃ vāpi (sī. syā.)</note> kathaṃ vibhoti;
```

```
Etaṃ me pabrūhi yathā vibhoti, taṃ jāniyāmāti <note>jānissāmāti (sī. ka.)</note> me mano ahu’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§880.</p>

```
‘‘Na saññasaññī na visaññasaññī, nopi asaññī na vibhūtasaññī;
```

```
Evaṃsametassa vibhoti rūpaṃ, saññānidānā hi papañcasaṅkhā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§881.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0415" /> taṃ apucchimha akittayī no,
```

```
Aññaṃ taṃ pucchāma tadiṅgha brūhi;
```

```
Ettāvataggaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0171" /> nu <note>no (sī. syā.)</note> vadanti heke,
```

```
Yakkhassa suddhiṃ idha paṇḍitāse;
```

```
Udāhu <pb ed="T" n="0.0505" /> aññampi vadanti etto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§882.</p>

```
‘‘Ettāvataggampi <pb ed="V" n="0.0213" /> vadanti heke, yakkhassa suddhiṃ idha paṇḍitāse;
```

```
Tesaṃ paneke samayaṃ vadanti, anupādisese kusalā vadānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§883.</p>

```
‘‘Ete ca ñatvā upanissitāti, ñatvā munī nissaye so vimaṃsī;
```

```
Ñatvā vimutto na vivādameti, bhavābhavāya na sameti dhīro’’ti.
```

Kalahavivādasuttaṃ ekādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 12. Cūḷabyūhasuttaṃ <note>cūḷaviyūhasuttaṃ (sī. syā. niddesa)</note>

<p rend="hangnum">§884.</p>

```
Sakaṃsakaṃdiṭṭhiparibbasānā, viggayha nānā kusalā vadanti;
```

```
Yo evaṃ jānāti sa vedi dhammaṃ, idaṃ paṭikkosamakevalī so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§885.</p>

```
Evampi viggayha vivādayanti, bālo paro akkusaloti <note>akusaloti (sī. syā. pī.)</note> cāhu;
```

```
Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaṃ, sabbeva <pb ed="T" n="0.0506" /> hīme kusalā vadānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§886.</p>

```
Parassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0416" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0172" /> ce dhammamanānujānaṃ, bālomako <note>bālo mago (sī. syā. ka.)</note> hoti nihīnapañño;
```

```
Sabbeva bālā sunihīnapaññā, sabbevime diṭṭhiparibbasānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§887.</p>

```
Sandiṭṭhiyā ceva na vīvadātā, saṃsuddhapaññā kusalā mutīmā;
```

```
Na tesaṃ koci parihīnapañño <note>kocipi nihīnapañño (sī. syā. ka.)</note>, diṭṭhī hi tesampi tathā samattā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§888.</p>

```
Na vāhametaṃ tathiyanti <note>tathivanti (syā. ka.)</note> brūmi, yamāhu bālā mithu aññamaññaṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃsakaṃdiṭṭhimakaṃsu saccaṃ, tasmā hi bāloti paraṃ dahanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§889.</p>

```
Yamāhu saccaṃ tathiyanti eke, tamāhu aññe <note>aññepi (syā.), aññe ca (?)</note> tucchaṃ musāti;
```

```
Evampi vigayha vivādayanti, kasmā na ekaṃ samaṇā vadanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§890.</p>

```
Ekañhi <pb ed="V" n="0.0214" /> saccaṃ na dutīyamatthi, yasmiṃ pajā no vivade pajānaṃ;
```

```
Nānā te <note>nānāto (ka.)</note> saccāni sayaṃ thunanti, tasmā <pb ed="T" n="0.0507" /> na ekaṃ samaṇā vadanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§891.</p>

```
Kasmā <pb ed="P" n="0.0173" /> nu saccāni vadanti nānā, pavādiyāse kusalā vadānā;
```

```
Saccāni sutāni bahūni nānā, udāhu te takkamanussaranti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§892.</p>

```
Na heva saccāni bahūni nānā, aññatra saññāya niccāni loke;
```

```
Takkañca diṭṭhīsu pakappayitvā, saccaṃ musāti dvayadhammamāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§893.</p>

```
Diṭṭhe <pb ed="M" n="0.0417" /> sute sīlavate mute vā, ete ca nissāya vimānadassī;
```

```
Vinicchaye ṭhatvā pahassamāno, bālo paro akkusaloti cāha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§894.</p>

```
Yeneva bāloti paraṃ dahāti, tenātumānaṃ kusaloti cāha;
```

```
Sayamattanā so kusalo vadāno, aññaṃ vimāneti tadeva pāva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§895.</p>

```
Atisāradiṭṭhiyāva so samatto, mānena matto paripuṇṇamānī;
```

```
Sayameva sāmaṃ manasābhisitto, diṭṭhī <pb ed="T" n="0.0508" /> hi sā tassa tathā samattā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§896.</p>

```
Parassa ce hi vacasā nihīno, tumo sahā hoti nihīnapañño;
```

```
Atha ce sayaṃ vedagū hoti dhīro, na koci bālo samaṇesu atthi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§897.</p>

```
Aññaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0174" /> ito yābhivadanti dhammaṃ, aparaddhā suddhimakevalī te <note>suddhimakevalīno (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Evampi titthyā puthuso vadanti, sandiṭṭhirāgena hi tebhirattā <note>tyābhirattā (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§898.</p>

```
Idheva suddhi iti vādayanti, nāññesu dhammesu visuddhimāhu;
```

```
Evampi titthyā puthuso niviṭṭhā, sakāyane tattha daḷhaṃ vadānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§899.</p>

```
Sakāyane vāpi daḷhaṃ vadāno, kamettha bāloti paraṃ daheyya;
```

```
Sayameva so medhagamāvaheyya <note>medhakaṃ āvaheyya (sī. pī.)</note>, paraṃ vadaṃ bālamasuddhidhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§900.</p>

```
Vinicchaye <pb ed="M" n="0.0418" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0215" /> ṭhatvā sayaṃ pamāya, uddhaṃ sa <note>uddaṃ so (sī. syā. pī.)</note> lokasmiṃ vivādameti;
```

```
Hitvāna sabbāni vinicchayāni, na <pb ed="T" n="0.0509" /> medhagaṃ kubbati jantu loketi.
```

Cūḷabyūhasuttaṃ dvādasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 13. Mahābyūhasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§901.</p>

```
Ye kecime diṭṭhiparibbasānā, idameva saccanti vivādayanti <note>vivādiyanti (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbeva te nindamanvānayanti, atho pasaṃsampi labhanti tattha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§902.</p>

```
Appañhi <pb ed="P" n="0.0175" /> etaṃ na alaṃ samāya, duve vivādassa phalāni brūmi;
```

```
Etampi disvā na vivādayetha, khemābhipassaṃ avivādabhūmiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§903.</p>

```
Yā kācimā sammutiyo puthujjā, sabbāva etā na upeti vidvā;
```

```
Anūpayo so upayaṃ kimeyya, diṭṭhe sute khantimakubbamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§904.</p>

```
Sīluttamā saññamenāhu suddhiṃ, vataṃ samādāya upaṭṭhitāse;
```

```
Idheva sikkhema athassa suddhiṃ, bhavūpanītā <pb ed="T" n="0.0510" /> kusalā vadānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§905.</p>

```
Sace cuto sīlavatato hoti, pavedhatī <note>sa vedhati (sī. pī.)</note> kamma virādhayitvā;
```

```
Pajappatī patthayatī ca suddhiṃ, satthāva hīno pavasaṃ gharamhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§906.</p>

```
Sīlabbataṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0419" /> vāpi pahāya sabbaṃ, kammañca sāvajjanavajjametaṃ;
```

```
Suddhiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0176" /> asuddhinti apatthayāno, virato care santimanuggahāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§907.</p>

```
Tamūpanissāya jigucchitaṃ vā, athavāpi diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
```

```
Uddhaṃsarā suddhimanutthunanti, avītataṇhāse bhavābhavesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§908.</p>

```
Patthayamānassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0216" /> hi jappitāni, pavedhitaṃ vāpi pakappitesu;
```

```
Cutūpapāto idha yassa natthi, sa kena vedheyya kuhiṃva jappe <note>kuhiñci jappe (sī. syā. ka.), kuhiṃ pajappe (pī.) niddeso passitabbo</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§909.</p>

```
Yamāhu dhammaṃ paramanti eke, tameva hīnanti panāhu aññe;
```

Sacco nu vādo katamo imesaṃ, sabbeva <pb ed="T" n="0.0511" /> hīme kusalā vadānā.

<p rend="hangnum">§910.</p>

```
Sakañhi dhammaṃ paripuṇṇamāhu, aññassa dhammaṃ pana hīnamāhu;
```

```
Evampi viggayha vivādayanti, sakaṃ sakaṃ sammutimāhu saccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§911.</p>

```
Parassa ce vambhayitena hīno, na koci dhammesu visesi assa;
```

```
Puthū hi aññassa vadanti dhammaṃ, nihīnato samhi daḷhaṃ vadānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§912.</p>

```
Saddhammapūjāpi <pb ed="P" n="0.0177" /> nesaṃ tatheva, yathā pasaṃsanti sakāyanāni;
```

```
Sabbeva vādā <note>sabbe pavādā (syā.)</note> tathiyā <note>tathivā (sabbattha)</note> bhaveyyuṃ, suddhī hi nesaṃ paccattameva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§913.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="0.0420" /> brāhmaṇassa paraneyyamatthi, dhammesu niccheyya samuggahītaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā vivādāni upātivatto, na hi seṭṭhato passati dhammamaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§914.</p>

```
Jānāmi passāmi tatheva etaṃ, diṭṭhiyā eke paccenti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Addakkhi ce kiñhi tumassa tena, atisitvā <pb ed="T" n="0.0512" /> aññena vadanti suddhiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§915.</p>

```
Passaṃ naro dakkhati <note>dakkhiti (sī.)</note> nāmarūpaṃ, disvāna vā ñassati tānimeva;
```

```
Kāmaṃ bahuṃ passatu appakaṃ vā, na hi tena suddhiṃ kusalā vadanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§916.</p>

```
Nivissavādī na hi subbināyo, pakappitaṃ diṭṭhi purekkharāno;
```

```
Yaṃ nissito tattha subhaṃ vadāno, suddhiṃvado tattha tathaddasā so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§917.</p>

```
Na brāhmaṇo kappamupeti saṅkhā <note>saṅkhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, na diṭṭhisārī napi ñāṇabandhu;
```

```
Ñatvā <pb ed="P" n="0.0178" /> ca so sammutiyo <note>sammatiyo (syā.)</note> puthujjā, upekkhatī uggahaṇanti maññe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§918.</p>

```
Vissajja <pb ed="V" n="0.0217" /> ganthāni munīdha loke, vivādajātesu na vaggasārī;
```

```
Santo asantesu upekkhako so, anuggaho uggahaṇanti maññe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§919.</p>

```
Pubbāsave hitvā nave akubbaṃ, na chandagū nopi nivissavādī;
```

```
Sa vippamutto diṭṭhigatehi dhīro, na <pb ed="T" n="0.0513" /> limpati <note>na lippati (sī. pī.)</note> loke anattagarahī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§920.</p>

```
Sa <pb ed="M" n="0.0421" /> sabbadhammesu visenibhūto, yaṃ kiñci diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā;
```

```
Sa pannabhāro muni vippamutto, na kappiyo nūparato na patthiyoti.
```

Mahābyūhasuttaṃ terasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 14. Tuvaṭakasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§921.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="P" n="0.0179" /> taṃ ādiccabandhu <note>ādiccabandhuṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, vivekaṃ santipadañca mahesi;
```

```
Kathaṃ disvā nibbāti bhikkhu, anupādiyāno lokasmiṃ kiñci’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§922.</p>

```
‘‘Mūlaṃ papañcasaṅkhāya, (iti bhagavā)
```

```
Mantā asmīti sabbamuparundhe <note>sabbamuparuddhe (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Yā kāci taṇhā ajjhattaṃ,
```

```
Tāsaṃ vinayā <note>vinayāya (?)</note> sadā sato sikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§923.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci dhammamabhijaññā, ajjhattaṃ athavāpi bahiddhā;
```

```
Na tena thāmaṃ <note>mānaṃ (sī. ka.)</note> kubbetha, na <pb ed="T" n="0.0514" /> hi sā nibbuti sataṃ vuttā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§924.</p>

```
‘‘Seyyo na tena maññeyya, nīceyyo athavāpi sarikkho;
```

```
Phuṭṭho <note>puṭṭho (sī. syā. ka.)</note> anekarūpehi, nātumānaṃ vikappayaṃ tiṭṭhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§925.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattamevupasame<pb ed="V" n="0.0218" />, na aññato bhikkhu santimeseyya;
```

```
Ajjhattaṃ upasantassa, natthi attā kuto nirattā vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§926.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhe <pb ed="M" n="0.0422" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0180" /> yathā samuddassa, ūmi no jāyatī ṭhito hoti;
```

```
Evaṃ ṭhito anejassa, ussadaṃ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§927.</p>

```
‘‘Akittayī vivaṭacakkhu, sakkhidhammaṃ parissayavinayaṃ;
```

```
Paṭipadaṃ vadehi bhaddante, pātimokkhaṃ athavāpi samādhiṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§928.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkhūhi neva lolassa, gāmakathāya āvaraye sotaṃ;
```

```
Rase ca nānugijjheyya, na <pb ed="T" n="0.0515" /> ca mamāyetha kiñci lokasmiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§929.</p>

```
‘‘Phassena yadā phuṭṭhassa, paridevaṃ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci;
```

```
Bhavañca nābhijappeyya, bheravesu ca na sampavedheyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§930.</p>

```
‘‘Annānamatho pānānaṃ, khādanīyānaṃ athopi vatthānaṃ;
```

```
Laddhā na sannidhiṃ kayirā, na ca parittase tāni alabhamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§931.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyī na pādalolassa, virame kukkuccā nappamajjeyya;
```

```
Athāsanesu sayanesu, appasaddesu bhikkhu vihareyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§932.</p>

```
‘‘Niddaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0181" /> na bahulīkareyya, jāgariyaṃ bhajeyya ātāpī;
```

```
Tandiṃ māyaṃ hassaṃ khiḍḍaṃ, methunaṃ vippajahe savibhūsaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§933.</p>

```
‘‘Āthabbaṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0423" /> supinaṃ lakkhaṇaṃ, no vidahe athopi nakkhattaṃ;
```

```
Virutañca gabbhakaraṇaṃ, tikicchaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0516" /> māmako na seveyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§934.</p>

```
‘‘Nindāya nappavedheyya, na uṇṇameyya pasaṃsito bhikkhu;
```

```
Lobhaṃ saha macchariyena, kodhaṃ pesuṇiyañca panudeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§935.</p>

```
‘‘Kayavikkaye <pb ed="V" n="0.0219" /> na tiṭṭheyya, upavādaṃ bhikkhu na kareyya kuhiñci;
```

```
Gāme ca nābhisajjeyya, lābhakamyā janaṃ na lapayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§936.</p>

```
‘‘Na ca katthitā siyā bhikkhu, na ca vācaṃ payuttaṃ bhāseyya;
```

```
Pāgabbhiyaṃ na sikkheyya, kathaṃ viggāhikaṃ na kathayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§937.</p>

```
‘‘Mosavajje na nīyetha, sampajāno saṭhāni na kayirā;
```

```
Atha <pb ed="P" n="0.0182" /> jīvitena paññāya, sīlabbatena nāññamatimaññe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§938.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā rusito bahuṃ vācaṃ, samaṇānaṃ vā puthujanānaṃ <note>puthuvacanānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pharusena ne na paṭivajjā, na <pb ed="T" n="0.0517" /> hi santo paṭisenikaronti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§939.</p>

```
‘‘Etañca dhammamaññāya, vicinaṃ bhikkhu sadā sato sikkhe;
```

```
Santīti nibbutiṃ ñatvā, sāsane gotamassa na pamajjeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§940.</p>

```
‘‘Abhibhū <pb ed="M" n="0.0424" /> hi so anabhibhūto, sakkhidhammamanītihamadassī;
```

```
Tasmā hi tassa bhagavato sāsane, appamatto sadā namassamanusikkhe’’ti.
```

Tuvaṭakasuttaṃ cuddasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 15. Attadaṇḍasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§941.</p>

```
‘‘Attadaṇḍā bhayaṃ jātaṃ, janaṃ passatha medhagaṃ;
```

```
Saṃvegaṃ kittayissāmi, yathā saṃvijitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§942.</p>

```
‘‘Phandamānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0183" /> pajaṃ disvā, macche appodake yathā;
```

```
Aññamaññehi byāruddhe, disvā maṃ bhayamāvisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§943.</p>

```
‘‘Samantamasāro <pb ed="V" n="0.0220" /> loko, disā sabbā sameritā;
```

```
Icchaṃ bhavanamattano, nāddasāsiṃ anositaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§944.</p>

```
‘‘Osānetveva <pb ed="T" n="0.0518" /> byāruddhe, disvā me aratī ahu;
```

```
Athettha sallamaddakkhiṃ, duddasaṃ hadayanissitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§945.</p>

```
‘‘Yena sallena otiṇṇo, disā sabbā vidhāvati;
```

```
Tameva sallamabbuyha, na dhāvati na sīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§946.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha sikkhānugīyanti <note>sikkhānukiriyanti (ka.)</note>, yāni loke gadhitāni;
```

```
Na tesu pasuto siyā, nibbijjha sabbaso kāme;
```

```
Sikkhe nibbānamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§947.</p>

```
‘‘Sacco siyā appagabbho, amāyo rittapesuṇo;
```

```
Akkodhano lobhapāpaṃ, vevicchaṃ vitare muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§948.</p>

```
‘‘Niddaṃ tandiṃ sahe thīnaṃ, pamādena na saṃvase;
```

```
Atimāne na tiṭṭheyya, nibbānamanaso naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§949.</p>

```
‘‘Mosavajje <pb ed="M" n="0.0425" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0184" /> na nīyetha, rūpe snehaṃ na kubbaye;
```

```
Mānañca parijāneyya, sāhasā virato care.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§950.</p>

```
‘‘Purāṇaṃ nābhinandeyya, nave khantiṃ na kubbaye;
```

```
Hiyyamāne na soceyya, ākāsaṃ na sito siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§951.</p>

```
‘‘Gedhaṃ brūmi mahoghoti, ājavaṃ brūmi jappanaṃ;
```

```
Ārammaṇaṃ pakappanaṃ, kāmapaṅko duraccayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§952.</p>

```
‘‘Saccā avokkamma <note>avokkamaṃ (niddesa)</note> muni, thale tiṭṭhati brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Sabbaṃ so <note>sabbaso (syā. ka.)</note> paṭinissajja, sa ve santoti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§953.</p>

```
‘‘Sa <pb ed="V" n="0.0221" /> ve vidvā sa vedagū, ñatvā dhammaṃ anissito;
```

```
Sammā <pb ed="T" n="0.0519" /> so loke iriyāno, na pihetīdha kassaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§954.</p>

```
‘‘Yodha kāme accatari, saṅgaṃ loke duraccayaṃ;
```

```
Na so socati nājjheti, chinnasoto abandhano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§955.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ pubbe taṃ visosehi, pacchā te māhu kiñcanaṃ;
```

```
Majjhe ce no gahessasi, upasanto carissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§956.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaso nāmarūpasmiṃ, yassa natthi mamāyitaṃ;
```

```
Asatā ca na socati, sa ve loke na jīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§957.</p>

```
‘‘Yassa natthi idaṃ meti, paresaṃ vāpi kiñcanaṃ;
```

```
Mamattaṃ so asaṃvindaṃ, natthi meti na socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§958.</p>

```
‘‘Aniṭṭhurī <pb ed="P" n="0.0185" /> ananugiddho, anejo sabbadhī samo;
```

```
Tamānisaṃsaṃ pabrūmi, pucchito avikampinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§959.</p>

```
‘‘Anejassa vijānato, natthi kāci nisaṅkhati <note>nisaṅkhiti (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

```
Virato so viyārabbhā, khemaṃ passati sabbadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§960.</p>

```
‘‘Na samesu na omesu, na ussesu vadate muni;
```

```
Santo so vītamaccharo, nādeti na nirassatī’’ti.
```

Attadaṇḍasuttaṃ pannarasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

#### 16. Sāriputtasuttaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§961.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="0.0426" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0222" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0520" /> me diṭṭho ito pubbe, (iccāyasmā sāriputto)
```

```
Na suto uda kassaci;
```

```
Evaṃ vagguvado satthā,
```

```
Tusitā gaṇimāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§962.</p>

```
‘‘Sadevakassa lokassa, yathā dissati cakkhumā;
```

```
Sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā, ekova ratimajjhagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§963.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0186" /> buddhaṃ asitaṃ tādiṃ, akuhaṃ gaṇimāgataṃ;
```

```
Bahūnamidha baddhānaṃ, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§964.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhuno vijigucchato, bhajato rittamāsanaṃ;
```

```
Rukkhamūlaṃ susānaṃ vā, pabbatānaṃ guhāsu vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§965.</p>

```
‘‘Uccāvacesu sayanesu, kīvanto tattha bheravā;
```

```
Yehi bhikkhu na vedheyya, nigghose sayanāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§966.</p>

```
‘‘Katī parissayā loke, gacchato agataṃ disaṃ;
```

```
Ye bhikkhu abhisambhave, pantamhi sayanāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§967.</p>

```
‘‘Kyāssa byappathayo assu, kyāssassu idha gocarā;
```

```
Kāni sīlabbatānāssu, pahitattassa bhikkhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§968.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṃ so sikkhaṃ samādāya, ekodi nipako sato;
```

```
Kammāro rajatasseva, niddhame malamattano’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§969.</p>

```
‘‘Vijigucchamānassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0223" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0521" /> yadidaṃ phāsu, (sāriputtāti bhagavā)
```

```
Rittāsanaṃ sayanaṃ sevato ce;
```

```
Sambodhikāmassa yathānudhammaṃ,
```

```
Taṃ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§970.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcannaṃ dhīro bhayānaṃ na bhāye, bhikkhu sato sapariyantacārī;
```

```
Ḍaṃsādhipātānaṃ sarīsapānaṃ, manussaphassānaṃ catuppadānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§971.</p>

```
‘‘Paradhammikānampi <pb ed="M" n="0.0427" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0187" /> na santaseyya, disvāpi tesaṃ bahubheravāni;
```

```
Athāparāni abhisambhaveyya, parissayāni kusalānuesī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§972.</p>

```
‘‘Ātaṅkaphassena khudāya phuṭṭho, sītaṃ atuṇhaṃ <note>accuṇhaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> adhivāsayeyya;
```

```
So tehi phuṭṭho bahudhā anoko, vīriyaṃ parakkammadaḷhaṃ kareyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§973.</p>

```
‘‘Theyyaṃ na kāre <note>na kareyya (sī. syā. ka.)</note> na musā bhaṇeyya, mettāya phasse tasathāvarāni;
```

```
Yadāvilattaṃ manaso vijaññā, kaṇhassa pakkhoti vinodayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§974.</p>

```
‘‘Kodhātimānassa <pb ed="T" n="0.0522" /> vasaṃ na gacche, mūlampi tesaṃ palikhañña tiṭṭhe;
```

```
Athappiyaṃ vā pana appiyaṃ vā, addhā bhavanto abhisambhaveyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§975.</p>

```
‘‘Paññaṃ purakkhatvā kalyāṇapīti, vikkhambhaye tāni parissayāni;
```

```
Aratiṃ sahetha sayanamhi pante, caturo sahetha paridevadhamme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§976.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃsū asissāmi kuvaṃ vā <note>kudha vā (ka.), kutha vā (niddesa)</note> asissaṃ, dukkhaṃ vata settha kvajja sessaṃ;
```

```
Ete vitakke paridevaneyye, vinayetha sekho aniketacārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§977.</p>

```
‘‘Annañca <pb ed="P" n="0.0188" /> laddhā vasanañca kāle, mattaṃ so jaññā idha tosanatthaṃ;
```

```
So tesu gutto yatacāri gāme, rusitopi vācaṃ pharusaṃ na vajjā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§978.</p>

```
‘‘Okkhittacakkhu <pb ed="M" n="0.0428" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0224" /> na ca pādalolo, jhānānuyutto bahujāgarassa;
```

```
Upekkhamārabbha samāhitatto, takkāsayaṃ kukkucciyūpachinde.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§979.</p>

```
‘‘Cudito <pb ed="T" n="0.0523" /> vacībhi satimābhinande, sabrahmacārīsu khilaṃ pabhinde;
```

```
Vācaṃ pamuñce kusalaṃ nātivelaṃ, janavādadhammāya na cetayeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§980.</p>

```
‘‘Athāparaṃ pañca rajāni loke, yesaṃ satīmā vinayāya sikkhe;
```

```
Rūpesu saddesu atho rasesu, gandhesu phassesu sahetha rāgaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§981.</p>

```
‘‘Etesu dhammesu vineyya chandaṃ, bhikkhu satimā suvimuttacitto;
```

```
Kālena <pb ed="P" n="0.0189" /> so sammā dhammaṃ parivīmaṃsamāno,
```

```
Ekodibhūto vihane tamaṃ so’’ti.
```

Sāriputtasuttaṃ soḷasamaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Aṭṭhakavaggo catuttho</trailer>

Niṭṭhito.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kāmaṃ guhañca duṭṭhā ca, suddhañca paramā jarā;
```

```
Metteyyo ca pasūro ca, māgaṇḍi purābhedanaṃ.
```

```
Kalahaṃ dve ca byūhāni <note>byūhāni (sī.)</note>, punadeva tuvaṭṭakaṃ;
```

```
Attadaṇḍavaraṃ suttaṃ, therapuṭṭhena <note>therapañhena (sī.), sāriputtena (syā.)</note> soḷasa;
```

```
Iti etāni suttāni, sabbānaṭṭhakavaggikāti.
```

### 5. Pārāyanavaggo

#### Vatthugāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§982.</p>

```
Kosalānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0429" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0225" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0190" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0524" /> purā rammā, agamā dakkhiṇāpathaṃ;
```

```
Ākiñcaññaṃ patthayāno, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§983.</p>

```
So assakassa visaye, aḷakassa <note>muḷakassa (syā.), mūḷhakassa (ka.), maḷakassa (niddesa)</note> samāsane;
```

```
Vasi godhāvarīkūle, uñchena ca phalena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§984.</p>

```
Tasseva upanissāya, gāmo ca vipulo ahu;
```

```
Tato jātena āyena, mahāyaññamakappayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§985.</p>

```
Mahāyaññaṃ yajitvāna, puna pāvisi assamaṃ;
```

```
Tasmiṃ paṭipaviṭṭhamhi, añño āgañchi brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§986.</p>

```
Ugghaṭṭapādo tasito <note>tassito (ka.)</note>, paṅkadanto rajassiro;
```

```
So ca naṃ upasaṅkamma, satāni pañca yācati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§987.</p>

```
Tamenaṃ bāvarī disvā, āsanena nimantayi;
```

```
Sukhañca kusalaṃ pucchi, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§988.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kho mama deyyadhammaṃ, sabbaṃ visajjitaṃ mayā;
```

```
Anujānāhi me brahme, natthi pañcasatāni me’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§989.</p>

```
‘‘Sace <pb ed="P" n="0.0191" /> me yācamānassa, bhavaṃ nānupadassati;
```

```
Sattame divase tuyhaṃ, muddhā phalatu sattadhā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§990.</p>

```
Abhisaṅkharitvā <pb ed="V" n="0.0226" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0525" /> kuhako, bheravaṃ so akittayi;
```

```
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, bāvarī dukkhito ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§991.</p>

```
Ussussati anāhāro, sokasallasamappito;
```

```
Athopi evaṃ cittassa, jhāne na ramatī mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§992.</p>

```
Utrastaṃ dukkhitaṃ disvā, devatā atthakāminī;
```

```
Bāvariṃ upasaṅkamma, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§993.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="0.0430" /> so muddhaṃ pajānāti, kuhako so dhanatthiko;
```

```
Muddhani muddhapāte vā, ñāṇaṃ tassa na vijjati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§994.</p>

```
‘‘Bhotī carahi jānāsi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchitā;
```

```
Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, taṃ suṇoma vaco tava’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§995.</p>

```
‘‘Ahampetaṃ na jānāmi, ñāṇamettha na vijjati;
```

```
Muddhani muddhādhipāte ca, jinānaṃ hettha <note>muddhaṃ muddhādhipāto ca, jinānaṃ heta (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dassanaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§996.</p>

```
‘‘Atha ko carahi jānāti, asmiṃ pathavimaṇḍale <note>puthavimaṇḍale (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, taṃ me akkhāhi devate’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§997.</p>

```
‘‘Purā <pb ed="P" n="0.0192" /> kapilavatthumhā, nikkhanto lokanāyako;
```

```
Apacco okkākarājassa, sakyaputto pabhaṅkaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§998.</p>

```
‘‘So hi brāhmaṇa sambuddho, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Sabbābhiññābalappatto, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
```

```
Sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto, vimutto upadhikkhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§999.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho so bhagavā loke, dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0526" /> tvaṃ gantvāna pucchassu, so te taṃ byākarissati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1000.</p>

```
Sambuddhoti <pb ed="V" n="0.0227" /> vaco sutvā, udaggo bāvarī ahu;
```

```
Sokassa tanuko āsi, pītiñca vipulaṃ labhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1001.</p>

```
So bāvarī attamano udaggo, taṃ devataṃ pucchati vedajāto;
```

```
‘‘Katamamhi gāme nigamamhi vā pana, katamamhi vā janapade lokanātho;
```

```
Yattha gantvāna passemu <note>gantvā namassemu (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, sambuddhaṃ dvipaduttamaṃ’’ <note>dvipaduttamaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>,.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1002.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvatthiyaṃ kosalamandire jino, pahūtapañño varabhūrimedhaso;
```

```
So sakyaputto vidhuro anāsavo, muddhādhipātassa vidū narāsabho’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1003.</p>

```
Tato <pb ed="M" n="0.0431" /> āmantayī sisse, brāhmaṇe mantapārage;
```

```
‘‘Etha māṇavā akkhissaṃ, suṇātha vacanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1004.</p>

```
‘‘Yasseso <pb ed="P" n="0.0193" /> dullabho loke, pātubhāvo abhiṇhaso;
```

```
Svājja lokamhi uppanno, sambuddho iti vissuto;
```

```
Khippaṃ gantvāna sāvatthiṃ, passavho dvipaduttamaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1005.</p>

```
‘‘Kathaṃ carahi jānemu, disvā buddhoti brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Ajānataṃ no pabrūhi, yathā jānemu taṃ mayaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1006.</p>

```
‘‘Āgatāni <pb ed="T" n="0.0527" /> hi mantesu, mahāpurisalakkhaṇā;
```

```
Dvattiṃsāni ca <note>dvittiṃsā ca (sī. syā. pī.), dvittiṃsa tāni (?)</note> byākkhātā, samattā anupubbaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1007.</p>

```
‘‘Yassete honti gattesu, mahāpurisalakkhaṇā;
```

```
Dveyeva tassa gatiyo, tatiyā hi na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1008.</p>

```
‘‘Sace agāraṃ āvasati <note>ajjhāvasati (ka.)</note>, vijeyya pathaviṃ imaṃ;
```

```
Adaṇḍena asatthena, dhammenamanusāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1009.</p>

```
‘‘Sace <pb ed="V" n="0.0228" /> ca so pabbajati, agārā anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Vivaṭṭacchado <note>vivattachaddo (sī.)</note> sambuddho, arahā bhavati anuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1010.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiṃ gottañca lakkhaṇaṃ, mante sisse punāpare;
```

```
Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, manasāyeva pucchatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1011.</p>

```
‘‘Anāvaraṇadassāvī, yadi buddho bhavissati;
```

```
Manasā pucchite pañhe, vācāya vissajessati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1012.</p>

```
Bāvarissa vaco sutvā, sissā soḷasa brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Ajito tissametteyyo, puṇṇako atha mettagū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1013.</p>

```
Dhotako <pb ed="P" n="0.0194" /> upasīvo ca, nando ca atha hemako;
```

```
Todeyyakappā dubhayo, jatukaṇṇī ca paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1014.</p>

```
Bhadrāvudho <pb ed="M" n="0.0432" /> udayo ca, posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Mogharājā ca medhāvī, piṅgiyo ca mahāisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1015.</p>

```
Paccekagaṇino sabbe, sabbalokassa vissutā;
```

```
Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā, pubbavāsanavāsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1016.</p>

```
Bāvariṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0528" /> abhivādetvā, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Jaṭājinadharā sabbe, pakkāmuṃ uttarāmukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1017.</p>

```
Aḷakassa patiṭṭhānaṃ, purimāhissatiṃ <note>purimaṃ māhissatiṃ (sī. pī.), puraṃ māhissatiṃ (syā.)</note> tadā;
```

```
Ujjeniñcāpi gonaddhaṃ, vedisaṃ vanasavhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1018.</p>

```
Kosambiñcāpi sāketaṃ, sāvatthiñca puruttamaṃ;
```

```
Setabyaṃ kapilavatthuṃ, kusinārañca mandiraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1019.</p>

```
Pāvañca <pb ed="V" n="0.0229" /> bhoganagaraṃ, vesāliṃ māgadhaṃ puraṃ;
```

```
Pāsāṇakaṃ cetiyañca, ramaṇīyaṃ manoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1020.</p>

```
Tasitovudakaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0195" /> sītaṃ, mahālābhaṃva vāṇijo;
```

```
Chāyaṃ ghammābhitattova, turitā pabbatamāruhuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1021.</p>

```
Bhagavā tamhi samaye, bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato;
```

```
Bhikkhūnaṃ dhammaṃ deseti, sīhova nadatī vane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1022.</p>

```
Ajito addasa buddhaṃ, sataraṃsiṃ <note>vītaraṃsiṃva (syā.), sataraṃsīva (ka.), pītaraṃsīva (niddesa)</note> va bhāṇumaṃ;
```

```
Candaṃ yathā pannarase, pāripūriṃ upāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1023.</p>

```
Athassa gatte disvāna, paripūrañca byañjanaṃ;
```

```
Ekamantaṃ ṭhito haṭṭho, manopañhe apucchatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1024.</p>

```
‘‘Ādissa jammanaṃ <note>jappanaṃ (ka.)</note> brūhi, gottaṃ brūhi salakkhaṇaṃ <note>brūhissa lakkhaṇaṃ (niddesa)</note>;
```

```
Mantesu pāramiṃ brūhi, kati vāceti brāhmaṇo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1025.</p>

```
‘‘Vīsaṃ vassasataṃ āyu, so ca gottena bāvarī;
```

```
Tīṇissa lakkhaṇā gatte, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1026.</p>

```
‘‘Lakkhaṇe <pb ed="M" n="0.0433" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0529" /> itihāse ca, sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe;
```

```
Pañcasatāni vāceti, sadhamme pāramiṃ gato’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1027.</p>

```
‘‘Lakkhaṇānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0196" /> pavicayaṃ, bāvarissa naruttama;
```

```
Kaṅkhacchida <note>taṇhacchida (bahūsu)</note> pakāsehi, mā no kaṅkhāyitaṃ ahu’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1028.</p>

```
‘‘Mukhaṃ jivhāya chādeti, uṇṇassa bhamukantare;
```

```
Kosohitaṃ vatthaguyhaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi māṇava’’.
```
