<p rend="hangnum">§1029.</p>

```
Pucchañhi <pb ed="V" n="0.0230" /> kiñci asuṇanto, sutvā pañhe viyākate;
```

```
Vicinteti jano sabbo, vedajāto katañjalī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1030.</p>

```
‘‘Ko nu devo vā brahmā vā, indo vāpi sujampati;
```

```
Manasā pucchite pañhe, kametaṃ paṭibhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1031.</p>

```
‘‘Muddhaṃ muddhādhipātañca, bāvarī paripucchati;
```

```
Taṃ byākarohi bhagavā, kaṅkhaṃ vinaya no ise’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1032.</p>

```
‘‘Avijjā muddhāti jānāhi, vijjā muddhādhipātinī;
```

```
Saddhāsatisamādhīhi, chandavīriyena saṃyutā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1033.</p>

```
Tato vedena mahatā, santhambhitvāna māṇavo;
```

```
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, pādesu sirasā pati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1034.</p>

```
‘‘Bāvarī brāhmaṇo bhoto, saha sissehi mārisa;
```

```
Udaggacitto sumano, pāde vandati cakkhuma’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1035.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhito <pb ed="P" n="0.0197" /> bāvarī hotu, saha sissehi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Tvañcāpi sukhito hohi, ciraṃ jīvāhi māṇava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1036.</p>

```
‘‘Bāvarissa <pb ed="T" n="0.0530" /> ca tuyhaṃ vā, sabbesaṃ sabbasaṃsayaṃ;
```

```
Katāvakāsā pucchavho, yaṃ kiñci manasicchatha’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1037.</p>

```
Sambuddhena katokāso, nisīditvāna pañjalī;
```

```
Ajito paṭhamaṃ pañhaṃ, tattha pucchi tathāgataṃ.
```

Vatthugāthā niṭṭhitā.

#### 1. Ajitamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1038.</p>

```
‘‘Kenassu <pb ed="M" n="0.0434" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0231" /> nivuto loko, (iccāyasmā ajito)
```

```
Kenassu nappakāsati;
```

```
Kissābhilepanaṃ brūsi, kiṃsu tassa mahabbhayaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1039.</p>

```
‘‘Avijjāya nivuto loko, (ajitāti bhagavā)
```

```
Vevicchā pamādā nappakāsati;
```

```
Jappābhilepanaṃ brūmi, dukkhamassa mahabbhayaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1040.</p>

```
‘‘Savanti <pb ed="P" n="0.0198" /> sabbadhi sotā, (iccāyasmā ajito)
```

```
Sotānaṃ kiṃ nivāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Sotānaṃ saṃvaraṃ brūhi, kena sotā pidhiyyare’’ <note>pithiyyare (sī. syā. pī.), pithīyare (sī. aṭṭha.), pidhīyare (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1041.</p>

```
‘‘Yāni sotāni lokasmiṃ, (ajitāti bhagavā)
```

```
Sati tesaṃ nivāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Sotānaṃ saṃvaraṃ brūmi, paññāyete pidhiyyare’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1042.</p>

```
‘‘Paññā ceva sati yañca <note>satī ceva (sī.), satī ca (syā.), satī cāpi (pī. niddesa), sati cāpi (niddesa)</note>, (iccāyasmā ajito)
```

```
Nāmarūpañca mārisa;
```

```
Etaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0531" /> me puṭṭho pabrūhi, katthetaṃ uparujjhati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1043.</p>

```
‘‘Yametaṃ pañhaṃ apucchi, ajita taṃ vadāmi te;
```

```
Yattha nāmañca rūpañca, asesaṃ uparujjhati;
```

```
Viññāṇassa nirodhena, etthetaṃ uparujjhati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1044.</p>

```
‘‘Ye ca saṅkhātadhammāse, ye ca sekhā puthū idha;
```

```
Tesaṃ me nipako iriyaṃ, puṭṭho pabrūhi mārisa’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1045.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmesu <pb ed="V" n="0.0232" /> nābhigijjheyya, manasānāvilo siyā;
```

```
Kusalo sabbadhammānaṃ, sato bhikkhu paribbaje’’ti.
```

Ajitamāṇavapucchā paṭhamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 2. Tissametteyyamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1046.</p>

```
‘‘Kodha <pb ed="M" n="0.0435" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0199" /> santusito loke, (iccāyasmā tissametteyyo)
```

```
Kassa no santi iñjitā;
```

```
Ko ubhantamabhiññāya, majjhe mantā na lippati <note>limpati (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Kaṃ brūsi mahāpurisoti, ko idha sibbinimaccagā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1047.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmesu brahmacariyavā, (metteyyāti bhagavā)
```

```
Vītataṇho sadā sato;
```

```
Saṅkhāya <pb ed="T" n="0.0532" /> nibbuto bhikkhu, tassa no santi iñjitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1048.</p>

```
‘‘So ubhantamabhiññāya, majjhe mantā na lippati;
```

```
Taṃ brūmi mahāpurisoti, so idha sibbinimaccagā’’ti.
```

Tissametteyyamāṇavapucchā dutiyā niṭṭhitā.

#### 3. Puṇṇakamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1049.</p>

```
‘‘Anejaṃ mūladassāviṃ, (iccāyasmā puṇṇako)
```

```
Atthi <note>atthī (syā.)</note> pañhena āgamaṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0233" /> nissitā <pb ed="P" n="0.0200" /> isayo manujā, khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṃ;
```

```
Yaññamakappayiṃsu puthūdha loke, pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1050.</p>

```
‘‘Ye kecime isayo manujā, (puṇṇakāti bhagavā)
```

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṃ;
```

```
Yaññamakappayiṃsu puthūdha loke, āsīsamānā puṇṇaka itthattaṃ <note>itthabhāvaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Jaraṃ sitā yaññamakappayiṃsu’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1051.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="M" n="0.0436" /> kecime isayo manujā, (iccāyasmā puṇṇako)
```

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā devatānaṃ;
```

```
Yaññamakappayiṃsu <pb ed="T" n="0.0533" /> puthūdha loke, kaccissu te bhagavā yaññapathe appamattā;
```

```
Atāruṃ jātiñca jarañca mārisa, pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1052.</p>

```
‘‘Āsīsanti thomayanti, abhijappanti juhanti; (Puṇṇakāti bhagavā)
```

```
Kāmābhijappanti paṭicca lābhaṃ, te yājayogā bhavarāgarattā;
```

```
Nātariṃsu jātijaranti brūmi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1053.</p>

```
‘‘Te <pb ed="P" n="0.0201" /> ce nātariṃsu yājayogā, (iccāyasmā puṇṇako)
```

```
Yaññehi jātiñca jarañca mārisa;
```

```
Atha ko carahi devamanussaloke, atāri jātiñca jarañca mārisa;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1054.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhāya lokasmi paroparāni <note>parovarāni (sī. syā.)</note>, (puṇṇakāti bhagavā)
```

```
Yassiñjitaṃ natthi kuhiñci loke;
```

```
Santo vidhūmo anīgho nirāso, atāri so jātijaranti brūmī’’ti.
```

Puṇṇakamāṇavapucchā tatiyā niṭṭhitā.

#### 4. Mettagūmāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1055.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi <pb ed="V" n="0.0234" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0534" /> taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ, (iccāyasmā mettagū)
```

```
Maññāmi taṃ vedaguṃ bhāvitattaṃ;
```

```
Kuto nu dukkhā samudāgatā ime, ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1056.</p>

```
‘‘Dukkhassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0437" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0202" /> ve maṃ pabhavaṃ apucchasi, (mettagūti bhagavā)
```

```
Taṃ te pavakkhāmi yathā pajānaṃ;
```

```
Upadhinidānā pabhavanti dukkhā, ye keci lokasmimanekarūpā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1057.</p>

```
‘‘Yo ve avidvā upadhiṃ karoti, punappunaṃ dukkhamupeti mando;
```

```
Tasmā pajānaṃ upadhiṃ na kayirā, dukkhassa jātippabhavānupassī’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1058.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ taṃ apucchimha akittayī no, aññaṃ taṃ pucchāma <note>pucchāmi (sī. pī.)</note> tadiṅgha brūhi;
```

```
Kathaṃ nu dhīrā vitaranti oghaṃ, jātiṃ jaraṃ sokapariddavañca;
```

```
Taṃ me muni sādhu viyākarohi, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1059.</p>

```
‘‘Kittayissāmi <pb ed="T" n="0.0535" /> te dhammaṃ, (mettagūti bhagavā)
```

```
Diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1060.</p>

```
‘‘Tañcāhaṃ abhinandāmi, mahesi dhammamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1061.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci sampajānāsi, (mettagūti bhagavā)
```

```
Uddhaṃ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe;
```

```
Etesu <pb ed="P" n="0.0203" /> nandiñca nivesanañca, panujja viññāṇaṃ bhave na tiṭṭhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1062.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃvihārī <pb ed="V" n="0.0235" /> sato appamatto, bhikkhu caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāni;
```

```
Jātiṃ jaraṃ sokapariddavañca, idheva vidvā pajaheyya dukkhaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1063.</p>

```
‘‘Etābhinandāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0438" /> vaco mahesino, sukittitaṃ gotamanūpadhīkaṃ;
```

```
Addhā hi bhagavā pahāsi dukkhaṃ, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1064.</p>

```
‘‘Te cāpi nūnappajaheyyu dukkhaṃ, ye tvaṃ muni aṭṭhitaṃ ovadeyya;
```

```
Taṃ taṃ namassāmi samecca nāga, appeva maṃ bhagavā aṭṭhitaṃ ovadeyya’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1065.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0536" /> brāhmaṇaṃ vedagumābhijaññā, akiñcanaṃ kāmabhave asattaṃ;
```

```
Addhā hi so oghamimaṃ atāri, tiṇṇo ca pāraṃ akhilo akaṅkho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1066.</p>

```
‘‘Vidvā ca yo <note>so (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vedagū naro idha, bhavābhave saṅgamimaṃ visajja;
```

```
So <pb ed="P" n="0.0204" /> vītataṇho anīgho nirāso, atāri so jātijaranti brūmī’’ti.
```

Mettagūmāṇavapucchā catutthī niṭṭhitā.

#### 5. Dhotakamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1067.</p>

```
‘‘Pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ, (iccāyasmā dhotako)
```

```
Vācābhikaṅkhāmi mahesi tuyhaṃ;
```

```
Tava sutvāna nigghosaṃ, sikkhe nibbānamattano’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1068.</p>

```
‘‘Tenahātappaṃ karohi, (dhotakāti bhagavā) idheva nipako sato;
```

```
Ito sutvāna nigghosaṃ, sikkhe nibbānamattano’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1069.</p>

```
‘‘Passāmahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0439" /> devamanussaloke, akiñcanaṃ brāhmaṇamiriyamānaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ taṃ namassāmi samantacakkhu, pamuñca <pb ed="T" n="0.0537" /> maṃ sakka kathaṃkathāhi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1070.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0236" /> sahissāmi <note>samissāmi (syā.), gamissāmi (sī.), samīhāmi (pī.)</note> pamocanāya, kathaṃkathiṃ dhotaka kañci loke;
```

```
Dhammañca seṭṭhaṃ abhijānamāno <note>ājānamāno (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, evaṃ tuvaṃ oghamimaṃ taresi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1071.</p>

```
‘‘Anusāsa brahme karuṇāyamāno, vivekadhammaṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ;
```

```
Yathāhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0205" /> ākāsova abyāpajjamāno, idheva santo asito careyyaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1072.</p>

```
‘‘Kittayissāmi te santiṃ, (dhotakāti bhagavā) diṭṭhe dhamme anītihaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1073.</p>

```
‘‘Tañcāhaṃ abhinandāmi, mahesi santimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1074.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ kiñci sampajānāsi, (dhotakāti bhagavā)
```

```
Uddhaṃ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe;
```

```
Etaṃ viditvā saṅgoti loke, bhavābhavāya mākāsi taṇha’’nti.
```

Dhotakamāṇavapucchā pañcamī niṭṭhitā.

#### 6. Upasīvamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1075.</p>

```
‘‘Eko <pb ed="T" n="0.0538" /> ahaṃ sakka mahantamoghaṃ, (iccāyasmā upasīvo)
```

```
Anissito no visahāmi tārituṃ;
```

```
Ārammaṇaṃ brūhi samantacakkhu, yaṃ nissito oghamimaṃ tareyyaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1076.</p>

```
‘‘Ākiñcaññaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0440" /> pekkhamāno satimā, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
```

```
Natthīti nissāya tarassu oghaṃ;
```

```
Kāme <pb ed="P" n="0.0206" /> pahāya virato kathāhi, taṇhakkhayaṃ nattamahābhipassa’’ <note>rattamahābhipassa (syā.), rattamahaṃ vipassa (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1077.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbesu <pb ed="V" n="0.0237" /> kāmesu yo vītarāgo, (iccāyasmā upasīvo)
```

```
Ākiñcaññaṃ nissito hitvā maññaṃ;
```

```
Saññāvimokkhe parame vimutto <note>dhimutto (ka.)</note>, tiṭṭhe nu so tattha anānuyāyī’’ <note>anānuvāyī (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1078.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbesu kāmesu yo vītarāgo, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
```

```
Ākiñcaññaṃ nissito hitvā maññaṃ;
```

```
Saññāvimokkhe parame vimutto, tiṭṭheyya so tattha anānuyāyī’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1079.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṭṭhe ce so tattha anānuyāyī, pūgampi <pb ed="T" n="0.0539" /> vassānaṃ samantacakkhu;
```

```
Tattheva so sītisiyā vimutto, cavetha viññāṇaṃ tathāvidhassa’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1080.</p>

```
‘‘Accī yathā vātavegena khittā <note>khittaṃ (syā.), khitto (pī.)</note>, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
```

```
Atthaṃ paleti na upeti saṅkhaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0207" /> munī nāmakāyā vimutto, atthaṃ paleti na upeti saṅkhaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1081.</p>

```
‘‘Atthaṅgato so uda vā so natthi, udāhu ve sassatiyā arogo;
```

```
Taṃ me munī sādhu viyākarohi, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1082.</p>

```
‘‘Atthaṅgatassa <pb ed="M" n="0.0441" /> na pamāṇamatthi, (upasīvāti bhagavā)
```

```
Yena naṃ vajjuṃ taṃ tassa natthi;
```

```
Sabbesu dhammesu samūhatesu, samūhatā vādapathāpi sabbe’’ti.
```

Upasīvamāṇavapucchā chaṭṭhī niṭṭhitā.

#### 7. Nandamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1083.</p>

```
‘‘Santi <pb ed="V" n="0.0238" /> loke munayo, (iccāyasmā nando)
```

```
Janā vadanti tayidaṃ kathaṃsu;
```

```
Ñāṇūpapannaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0540" /> no muniṃ <note>muni no (syā. ka.)</note> vadanti, udāhu ve jīvitenūpapannaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1084.</p>

```
‘‘Na diṭṭhiyā na sutiyā na ñāṇena, (na sīlabbatena) <note>( ) natthi sī.-pī potthakesu</note>
```

```
Munīdha nanda kusalā vadanti;
```

```
Visenikatvā <pb ed="P" n="0.0208" /> anīghā nirāsā, caranti ye te munayoti brūmi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1085.</p>

```
‘‘Ye kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (iccāyasmā nando)
```

```
Diṭṭhassutenāpi <note>diṭṭhena sutenāpi (sī.), diṭṭhe sutenāpi (syā. pī. ka.)</note> vadanti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ, anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Kaccissu te bhagavā tattha yatā carantā, atāru jātiñca jarañca mārisa;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1086.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="M" n="0.0442" /> kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (nandāti bhagavā)
```

```
Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ, anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Kiñcāpi te tattha yatā caranti, nāriṃsu jātijaranti brūmi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1087.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="T" n="0.0541" /> kecime samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (iccāyasmā nando)
```

```
Diṭṭhassutenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Sīlabbatenāpi vadanti suddhiṃ, anekarūpena vadanti suddhiṃ;
```

```
Te ce muni <note>sace muni (sī.)</note> brūsi anoghatiṇṇe, atha <pb ed="P" n="0.0209" /> ko carahi devamanussaloke;
```

```
Atāri jātiñca jarañca mārisa, pucchāmi taṃ bhagavā brūhi me taṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1088.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ sabbe samaṇabrāhmaṇāse, (nandāti bhagavā)
```

```
Jātijarāya nivutāti brūmi;
```

```
Ye <pb ed="V" n="0.0239" /> sīdha diṭṭhaṃva sutaṃ mutaṃ vā, sīlabbataṃ vāpi pahāya sabbaṃ;
```

```
Anekarūpampi pahāya sabbaṃ, taṇhaṃ pariññāya anāsavāse;
```

```
Te ve narā oghatiṇṇāti brūmi’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1089.</p>

```
‘‘Etābhinandāmi vaco mahesino, sukittitaṃ gotamanūpadhīkaṃ;
```

```
Ye sīdha diṭṭhaṃ va sutaṃ mutaṃ vā, sīlabbataṃ vāpi pahāya sabbaṃ;
```

```
Anekarūpampi <pb ed="T" n="0.0542" /> pahāya sabbaṃ, taṇhaṃ pariññāya anāsavāse;
```

```
Ahampi te oghatiṇṇāti brūmī’’ti.
```

Nandamāṇavapucchā sattamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 8. Hemakamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1090.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="M" n="0.0443" /> me pubbe viyākaṃsu, (iccāyasmā hemako)
```

```
Huraṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0210" /> gotamasāsanā;
```

```
Iccāsi iti bhavissati, sabbaṃ taṃ itihītihaṃ;
```

```
Sabbaṃ taṃ takkavaḍḍhanaṃ, nāhaṃ tattha abhiramiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1091.</p>

```
‘‘Tvañca me dhammamakkhāhi, taṇhānigghātanaṃ muni;
```

```
Yaṃ viditvā sato caraṃ, tare loke visattikaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1092.</p>

```
‘‘Idha diṭṭhasutamutaviññātesu, piyarūpesu hemaka;
```

```
Chandarāgavinodanaṃ, nibbānapadamaccutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1093.</p>

```
‘‘Etadaññāya ye satā, diṭṭhadhammābhinibbutā;
```

```
Upasantā ca te sadā, tiṇṇā loke visattika’’nti.
```

Hemakamāṇavapucchā aṭṭhamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 9. Todeyyamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1094.</p>

```
‘‘Yasmiṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0240" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0543" /> kāmā na vasanti, (iccāyasmā todeyyo)
```

```
Taṇhā yassa na vijjati;
```

```
Kathaṃkathā ca yo tiṇṇo, vimokkho tassa kīdiso’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1095.</p>

```
‘‘Yasmiṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0211" /> kāmā na vasanti, (todeyyāti bhagavā)
```

```
Taṇhā yassa na vijjati;
```

```
Kathaṃkathā ca yo tiṇṇo, vimokkho tassa nāparo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1096.</p>

```
‘‘Nirāsaso so uda āsasāno, paññāṇavā so uda paññakappī;
```

```
Muniṃ ahaṃ sakka yathā vijaññaṃ, taṃ me viyācikkha samantacakkhu’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1097.</p>

```
‘‘Nirāsaso <pb ed="M" n="0.0444" /> so na ca āsasāno, paññāṇavā so na ca paññakappī;
```

```
Evampi todeyya muniṃ vijāna, akiñcanaṃ kāmabhave asatta’’nti.
```

Todeyyamāṇavapucchā navamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 10. Kappamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1098.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhe <pb ed="T" n="0.0544" /> sarasmiṃ tiṭṭhataṃ, (iccāyasmā kappo)
```

```
Oghe jāte mahabbhaye;
```

```
Jarāmaccuparetānaṃ, dīpaṃ pabrūhi mārisa;
```

```
Tvañca me dīpamakkhāhi, yathāyidaṃ nāparaṃ siyā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1099.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhe <pb ed="V" n="0.0241" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0212" /> sarasmiṃ tiṭṭhataṃ, (kappāti bhagavā)
```

```
Oghe jāte mahabbhaye;
```

```
Jarāmaccuparetānaṃ, dīpaṃ pabrūmi kappa te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1100.</p>

```
‘‘Akiñcanaṃ anādānaṃ, etaṃ dīpaṃ anāparaṃ;
```

```
Nibbānaṃ iti <note>nibbānamīti (sī.)</note> naṃ brūmi, jarāmaccuparikkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1101.</p>

```
‘‘Etadaññāya ye satā, diṭṭhadhammābhinibbutā;
```

```
Na te māravasānugā, na te mārassa paddhagū’’ti <note>paṭṭhagūti (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

Kappamāṇavapucchā dasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 11. Jatukaṇṇimāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1102.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvānahaṃ vīramakāmakāmiṃ, (iccāyasmā jatukaṇṇi)
```

```
Oghātigaṃ puṭṭhumakāmamāgamaṃ;
```

```
Santipadaṃ brūhi sahajanetta, yathātacchaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0545" /> bhagavā brūhi me taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1103.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā <pb ed="M" n="0.0445" /> hi kāme abhibhuyya iriyati, ādiccova pathaviṃ tejī tejasā;
```

```
Parittapaññassa me bhūripañña, ācikkha dhammaṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ;
```

```
Jātijarāya idha vippahānaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1104.</p>

```
‘‘Kāmesu <pb ed="P" n="0.0213" /> vinaya gedhaṃ, (jatukaṇṇīti bhagavā) nekkhammaṃ daṭṭhu khemato;
```

```
Uggahītaṃ nirattaṃ vā, mā te vijjittha kiñcanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1105.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ pubbe taṃ visosehi, pacchā te māhu kiñcanaṃ;
```

```
Majjhe ce no gahessasi, upasanto carissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1106.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaso <pb ed="V" n="0.0242" /> nāmarūpasmiṃ, vītagedhassa brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Āsavāssa na vijjanti, yehi maccuvasaṃ vaje’’ti.
```

Jatukaṇṇimāṇavapucchā ekādasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 12. Bhadrāvudhamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1107.</p>

```
‘‘Okañjahaṃ taṇhacchidaṃ anejaṃ, (iccāyasmā bhadrāvudho)
```

```
Nandiñjahaṃ oghatiṇṇaṃ vimuttaṃ;
```

```
Kappañjahaṃ abhiyāce sumedhaṃ, sutvāna <pb ed="T" n="0.0546" /> nāgassa apanamissanti ito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1108.</p>

```
‘‘Nānājanā janapadehi saṅgatā, tava vīra vākyaṃ abhikaṅkhamānā;
```

```
Tesaṃ tuvaṃ sādhu viyākarohi, tathā hi te vidito esa dhammo’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1109.</p>

```
‘‘Ādānataṇhaṃ vinayetha sabbaṃ, (bhadrāvudhāti bhagavā)
```

```
Uddhaṃ adho tiriyañcāpi majjhe;
```

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0214" /> yañhi lokasmimupādiyanti, teneva māro anveti jantuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1110.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmā <pb ed="M" n="0.0446" /> pajānaṃ na upādiyetha, bhikkhu sato kiñcanaṃ sabbaloke;
```

```
Ādānasatte iti pekkhamāno, pajaṃ imaṃ maccudheyye visatta’’nti.
```

Bhadrāvudhamāṇavapucchā dvādasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 13. Udayamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1111.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyiṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0243" /> virajamāsīnaṃ, (iccāyasmā udayo) katakiccaṃ anāsavaṃ;
```

```
Pāraguṃ sabbadhammānaṃ, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ;
```

```
Aññāvimokkhaṃ pabrūhi, avijjāya pabhedanaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1112.</p>

```
‘‘Pahānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0547" /> kāmacchandānaṃ, (udayāti bhagavā) domanassāna cūbhayaṃ;
```

```
Thinassa ca panūdanaṃ, kukkuccānaṃ nivāraṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1113.</p>

```
‘‘Upekkhāsatisaṃsuddhaṃ, dhammatakkapurejavaṃ;
```

```
Aññāvimokkhaṃ pabrūmi, avijjāya pabhedanaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1114.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃsu <pb ed="P" n="0.0215" /> saṃyojano loko, kiṃsu tassa vicāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Kissassa vippahānena, nibbānaṃ iti vuccati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1115.</p>

```
‘‘Nandisaṃyojano loko, vitakkassa vicāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Taṇhāya vippahānena, nibbānaṃ iti vuccati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1116.</p>

```
‘‘Kathaṃ satassa carato, viññāṇaṃ uparujjhati;
```

```
Bhagavantaṃ puṭṭhumāgamma, taṃ suṇoma vaco tava’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1117.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, vedanaṃ nābhinandato;
```

```
Evaṃ satassa carato, viññāṇaṃ uparujjhatī’’ti.
```

Udayamāṇavapucchā terasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 14. Posālamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1118.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="M" n="0.0447" /><pb ed="V" n="0.0244" /> atītaṃ ādisati, (iccāyasmā posālo) anejo chinnasaṃsayo;
```

```
Pāraguṃ sabbadhammānaṃ, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1119.</p>

```
‘‘Vibhūtarūpasaññissa<pb ed="T" n="0.0548" />, sabbakāyappahāyino;
```

```
Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, natthi kiñcīti passato;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ sakkānupucchāmi, kathaṃ neyyo tathāvidho’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1120.</p>

```
‘‘Viññāṇaṭṭhitiyo <pb ed="P" n="0.0216" /> sabbā, (posālāti bhagavā) abhijānaṃ tathāgato;
```

```
Tiṭṭhantamenaṃ jānāti, vimuttaṃ tapparāyaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1121.</p>

```
‘‘Ākiñcaññasambhavaṃ ñatvā, nandī saṃyojanaṃ iti;
```

```
Evametaṃ abhiññāya, tato tattha vipassati;
```

```
Etaṃ <note>evaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> ñāṇaṃ tathaṃ tassa, brāhmaṇassa vusīmato’’ti.
```

Posālamāṇavapucchā cuddasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 15. Mogharājamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1122.</p>

```
‘‘Dvāhaṃ sakkaṃ apucchissaṃ, (iccāyasmā mogharājā)
```

```
Na me byākāsi cakkhumā;
```

```
Yāvatatiyañca devīsi, byākarotīti me sutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1123.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ loko paro loko, brahmaloko sadevako;
```

```
Diṭṭhiṃ te nābhijānāti, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1124.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="0.0245" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0217" /><pb ed="T" n="0.0549" /> abhikkantadassāviṃ, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ;
```

```
Kathaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ, maccurājā na passati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1125.</p>

```
‘‘Suññato <pb ed="M" n="0.0448" /> lokaṃ avekkhassu, mogharāja sadā sato;
```

```
Attānudiṭṭhiṃ ūhacca, evaṃ maccutaro siyā;
```

```
Evaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ, maccurājā na passatī’’ti.
```

Mogharājamāṇavapucchā pannarasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### 16. Piṅgiyamāṇavapucchā

<p rend="hangnum">§1126.</p>

```
‘‘Jiṇṇohamasmi abalo vītavaṇṇo, (iccāyasmā piṅgiyo)
```

```
Nettā na suddhā savanaṃ na phāsu;
```

```
Māhaṃ nassaṃ momuho antarāva
```

```
Ācikkha dhammaṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ;
```

```
Jātijarāya idha vippahānaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1127.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna rūpesu vihaññamāne, (piṅgiyāti bhagavā)
```

```
Ruppanti rūpesu janā pamattā;
```

```
Tasmā tuvaṃ piṅgiya appamatto,
```

```
Jahassu rūpaṃ apunabbhavāya’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1128.</p>

```
‘‘Disā catasso vidisā catasso, uddhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="0.0550" /> adho dasa disā imāyo;
```

```
Na <pb ed="P" n="0.0218" /> tuyhaṃ adiṭṭhaṃ asutaṃ amutaṃ <note>asutaṃ amutaṃ vā (sī.), asutāmutaṃ vā (syā.), asutaṃ’mutaṃ vā (pī.)</note>, atho aviññātaṃ kiñcanamatthi <note>kiñci matthi (syā.), kiñci natthi (pī.), kiñcinamatthi (ka.)</note> loke;
```

```
Ācikkha dhammaṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ, jātijarāya idha vippahānaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1129.</p>

```
‘‘Taṇhādhipanne <pb ed="V" n="0.0246" /> manuje pekkhamāno, (piṅgiyāti bhagavā)
```

```
Santāpajāte jarasā parete;
```

```
Tasmā tuvaṃ piṅgiya appamatto, jahassu taṇhaṃ apunabbhavāyā’’ti.
```

Piṅgiyamāṇavapucchā soḷasamā niṭṭhitā.

#### Pārāyanatthutigāthā

Idamavoca <pb ed="M" n="0.0449" /> bhagavā magadhesu viharanto pāsāṇake cetiye, paricārakasoḷasānaṃ <note>paricārakasoḷasannaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> brāhmaṇānaṃ ajjhiṭṭho puṭṭho puṭṭho pañhaṃ <note>pañhe (sī. pī.)</note> byākāsi. Ekamekassa cepi pañhassa atthamaññāya dhammamaññāya dhammānudhammaṃ paṭipajjeyya, gaccheyyeva jarāmaraṇassa pāraṃ. Pāraṅgamanīyā ime dhammāti, tasmā imassa dhammapariyāyassa pārāyananteva <note>pārāyaṇaṃtveva (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> adhivacanaṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§1130.</p>

```
Ajito tissametteyyo, puṇṇako atha mettagū;
```

```
Dhotako upasīvo ca, nando ca atha hemako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1131.</p>

```
Todeyya-kappā <pb ed="P" n="0.0219" /> dubhayo, jatukaṇṇī ca paṇḍito;
```

```
Bhadrāvudho udayo ca, posālo cāpi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Mogharājā <pb ed="T" n="0.0551" /> ca medhāvī, piṅgiyo ca mahāisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1132.</p>

```
Ete buddhaṃ upāgacchuṃ, sampannacaraṇaṃ isiṃ;
```

```
Pucchantā nipuṇe pañhe, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1133.</p>

```
Tesaṃ buddho pabyākāsi, pañhe puṭṭho yathātathaṃ;
```

```
Pañhānaṃ veyyākaraṇena, tosesi brāhmaṇe muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1134.</p>

```
Te tositā cakkhumatā, buddhenādiccabandhunā;
```

```
Brahmacariyamacariṃsu, varapaññassa santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1135.</p>

```
Ekamekassa <pb ed="V" n="0.0247" /> pañhassa, yathā buddhena desitaṃ;
```

```
Tathā yo paṭipajjeyya, gacche pāraṃ apārato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1136.</p>

```
Apārā pāraṃ gaccheyya, bhāvento maggamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Maggo so pāraṃ gamanāya, tasmā pārāyanaṃ iti.
```

#### Pārāyanānugītigāthā

<p rend="hangnum">§1137.</p>

```
‘‘Pārāyanamanugāyissaṃ, (iccāyasmā piṅgiyo)
```

```
Yathāddakkhi tathākkhāsi, vimalo bhūrimedhaso;
```

```
Nikkāmo nibbano <note>nibbuto (syā.)</note> nāgo, kissa hetu musā bhaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1138.</p>

```
‘‘Pahīnamalamohassa<pb ed="M" n="0.0450" /><pb ed="P" n="0.0220" />, mānamakkhappahāyino;
```

```
Handāhaṃ kittayissāmi, giraṃ vaṇṇūpasañhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1139.</p>

```
‘‘Tamonudo buddho samantacakkhu, lokantagū sabbabhavātivatto;
```

```
Anāsavo sabbadukkhapahīno, saccavhayo <pb ed="T" n="0.0552" /> brahme upāsito me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1140.</p>

```
‘‘Dijo yathā kubbanakaṃ pahāya, bahupphalaṃ kānanamāvaseyya;
```

```
Evaṃ pahaṃ appadasse pahāya, mahodadhiṃ haṃsoriva ajjhapatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1141.</p>

```
‘‘Yeme pubbe viyākaṃsu, huraṃ gotamasāsanā;
```

```
Iccāsi iti bhavissati;
```

```
Sabbaṃ taṃ itihitihaṃ, sabbaṃ taṃ takkavaḍḍhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1142.</p>

```
‘‘Eko tamanudāsino, jutimā so pabhaṅkaro;
```

```
Gotamo bhūripaññāṇo, gotamo bhūrimedhaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1143.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="P" n="0.0221" /> me dhammamadesesi, sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṃ;
```

```
Taṇhakkhayamanītikaṃ<pb ed="T" n="0.0553" />, yassa natthi upamā kvaci’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1144.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃnu <pb ed="V" n="0.0248" /> tamhā vippavasasi, muhuttamapi piṅgiya;
```

```
Gotamā bhūripaññāṇā, gotamā bhūrimedhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1145.</p>

```
‘‘Yo te dhammamadesesi, sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṃ;
```

```
Taṇhakkhayamanītikaṃ, yassa natthi upamā kvaci’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1146.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ tamhā vippavasāmi, muhuttamapi brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Gotamā bhūripaññāṇā, gotamā bhūrimedhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1147.</p>

```
‘‘Yo me dhammamadesesi, sandiṭṭhikamakālikaṃ;
```

```
Taṇhakkhayamanītikaṃ, yassa natthi upamā kvaci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1148.</p>

```
‘‘Passāmi <pb ed="M" n="0.0451" /> naṃ manasā cakkhunāva, rattindivaṃ brāhmaṇa appamatto;
```

```
Namassamāno vivasemi rattiṃ, teneva maññāmi avippavāsaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1149.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhā ca pīti ca mano sati ca, nāpenti me gotamasāsanamhā;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ disaṃ vajati bhūripañño, sa tena teneva natohamasmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1150.</p>

```
‘‘Jiṇṇassa <pb ed="P" n="0.0222" /> me dubbalathāmakassa, teneva kāyo na paleti tattha;
```

```
Saṃkappayantāya <note>saṃkappayattāya (sī.)</note> vajāmi niccaṃ, mano hi me brāhmaṇa tena yutto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1151.</p>

```
‘‘Paṅke sayāno pariphandamāno, dīpā dīpaṃ upaplaviṃ <note>upallaviṃ (syā. niddesa)</note>;
```

```
Athaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1152.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā ahū vakkali muttasaddho, bhadrāvudho āḷavi gotamo ca;
```

```
Evameva tvampi pamuñcassu saddhaṃ,
```

```
Gamissasi tvaṃ piṅgiya maccudheyyassa pāraṃ’’ <note>maccudheyyapāraṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1153.</p>

```
‘‘Esa bhiyyo pasīdāmi, sutvāna munino vaco;
```

```
Vivaṭṭacchado <pb ed="T" n="0.0554" /> sambuddho, akhilo paṭibhānavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1154.</p>

```
‘‘Adhideve <pb ed="V" n="0.0249" /> abhiññāya, sabbaṃ vedi varovaraṃ <note>paro varaṃ (sī. syā.), paro paraṃ (niddesa)</note>;
```

```
Pañhānantakaro satthā, kaṅkhīnaṃ paṭijānataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§1155.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṃhīraṃ <pb ed="P" n="0.0223" /> asaṅkuppaṃ, yassa natthi upamā kvaci;
```

```
Addhā gamissāmi na mettha kaṅkhā, evaṃ maṃ dhārehi adhimuttacitta’’nti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Pārāyanavaggo pañcamo niṭṭhito.</trailer>

Suttuddānaṃ –

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Urago <pb ed="M" n="0.0452" /> <note>imā uddānagāthāyo sī. pī. potthakesu na santi</note> dhaniyopi ca, khaggavisāṇo kasi ca;
```

```
Cundo bhavo punadeva, vasalo ca karaṇīyañca;
```

```
Hemavato atha yakkho, vijayasuttaṃ munisuttavaranti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Paṭhamakaṭṭhavaro varavaggo, dvādasasuttadharo suvibhatto;
```

```
Desito cakkhumatā vimalena, suyyati vaggavaro uragoti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Ratanāmagandho hirimaṅgalanāmo, sucilomakapilo ca brāhmaṇadhammo;
```

```
Nāvā <note>nātha (ka.)</note> kiṃsīlauṭṭhahano ca, rāhulo <pb ed="T" n="0.0555" /> ca punapi vaṅgīso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Sammāparibbājanīyopi cettha, dhammikasuttavaro suvibhatto;
```

```
Cuddasasuttadharo dutiyamhi, cūḷakavaggavaroti tamāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Pabbajjapadhānasubhāsitanāmo, pūraḷāso punadeva māgho ca;
```

```
Sabhiyaṃ keṇiyameva sallanāmo, vāseṭṭhavaro kālikopi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Nālakasuttavaro suvibhatto, taṃ anupassī tathā punadeva;
```

```
Dvādasasuttadharo tatiyamhi, suyyati vaggavaro mahānāmo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Kāmaguhaṭṭhakaduṭṭhakanāmā<pb ed="V" n="0.0250" />, suddhavaro paramaṭṭhakanāmo;
```

```
Jarā mettiyavaro suvibhatto, pasūramāgaṇḍiyā purābhedo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Kalahavivādo <pb ed="M" n="0.0453" /> ubho viyuhā ca, tuvaṭakaattadaṇḍasāriputtā;
```

```
Soḷasasuttadharo catutthamhi, aṭṭhakavaggavaroti <pb ed="T" n="0.0556" /> tamāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Magadhe janapade ramaṇīye, desavare katapuññanivese;
```

```
Pāsāṇakacetiyavare suvibhatte, vasi bhagavā gaṇaseṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Ubhayavāsamāgatiyamhi <note>ubhayaṃ vā puṇṇasamāgataṃ yamhi (syā.)</note>, dvādasayojaniyā parisāya;
```

```
Soḷasabrāhmaṇānaṃ kira puṭṭho, pucchāya soḷasapañhakammiyā;
```

```
Nippakāsayi dhammamadāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Atthapakāsakabyañjanapuṇṇaṃ, dhammamadesesi parakhemajaniyaṃ <note>varaṃ khamanīyaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Lokahitāya jino dvipadaggo, suttavaraṃ bahudhammavicitraṃ;
```

```
Sabbakilesapamocanahetuṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Byañjanamatthapadaṃ samayuttaṃ <note>byañjanamatthapadasamayuttaṃ (syā.)</note>, akkharasaññitaopamagāḷhaṃ;
```

```
Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Rāgamale <pb ed="T" n="0.0557" /> amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ, dosamale amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ;
```

```
Mohamale amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ, lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ;
```

```
Desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Klesamale <pb ed="M" n="0.0454" /> amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ, duccaritamale amalaṃ vimalaggaṃ;
```

```
Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Āsavabandhanayogākilesaṃ, nīvaraṇāni ca tīṇi malāni;
```

```
Tassa kilesapamocanahetuṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Nimmalasabbakilesapanūdaṃ, rāgavirāgamanejamasokaṃ;
```

```
Santapaṇītasududdasadhammaṃ, desayi <pb ed="T" n="0.0558" /> suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Rāgañca <pb ed="V" n="0.0251" /> dosakamabhañjitasantaṃ <note>dosañca bhañjitasantaṃ (syā.)</note>, yonicatuggatipañcaviññāṇaṃ;
```

```
Taṇhāratacchadanatāṇalatāpamokkhaṃ <note>taṇhātalaratacchedanatāṇapamokkhaṃ (syā.)</note>, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Gambhīraduddasasaṇhanipuṇaṃ, paṇḍitavedaniyaṃ nipuṇatthaṃ;
```

```
Lokavicāraṇañāṇapabhaggaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Navaṅgakusumamālagīveyyaṃ, indriyajhānavimokkhavibhattaṃ;
```

```
Aṭṭhaṅgamaggadharaṃ varayānaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Somupamaṃ <pb ed="M" n="0.0455" /> vimalaṃ parisuddhaṃ, aṇṇavamūpamaratanasucittaṃ;
```

```
Pupphasamaṃ ravimūpamatejaṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Khemasivaṃ sukhasītalasantaṃ, maccutatāṇaparaṃ paramatthaṃ;
```

```
Tassa sunibbutadassanahetuṃ, desayi suttavaraṃ dvipadaggoti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Suttanipātapāḷi niṭṭhitā.</trailer>
